# WinUI 3 parity sweep — verified findings & execution plan

Generated 2026-06-11 from the `winui-parity-sweep` workflow: 40 finder agents (one per control
family + 5 systemic audits) compared every control in `src/FluentGpu.Controls` against the WinUI 3
sources at `C:\WAVEE\microsoft-ui-xaml` (behavior `.cpp/.h/.idl`, templates `.xaml`,
`_themeresources.xaml`), each followed by an adversarial verifier that re-opened every cited file
and refuted anything that didn't reproduce. **732 findings confirmed, 2 refuted** (86 agents,
~1,700 file reads). Every numeric/color/name claim below carries `path:line` evidence on both
sides; nothing is from memory.

> **Note (paths updated for the 2026-06 project consolidation):** `path:line` citations in the
> findings below use the pre-consolidation paths (e.g. `src/FluentGpu.Reconciler/Reconciler.cs`,
> `src/FluentGpu.Input/InputDispatcher.cs`, `src/FluentGpu.Dsl/Element.cs`). Map them to the
> consolidated layout: engine-layer files now live under `src/FluentGpu.Engine/<folder>/`
> (e.g. `src/FluentGpu.Engine/Reconciler/Reconciler.cs`); Windows-backend files live under
> `src/FluentGpu.Windows/<folder>/`. Namespaces and type names are unchanged.

Methodology and conventions live in `docs/guide/winui-control-parity-audit.md` (three source
layers: themeresources, behavior cpp, generated TemplateSettings). This document is the
work-planning output: what differs, exactly, and in what order to fix it.

## Reading the findings

- Format: `[severity|kind] Title — ours: <value> (path:line) vs WinUI: <value> (path:line). Fix: <exact change>.`
- Kinds: `missing-api`, `missing-behavior`, `styling-delta`, `motion-delta`, `bug`, `engine-gap`, `improvement`.
- `(ENGINE)` = needs an engine change (Reconciler/InputDispatcher/Layout/Text/Render), per the
  root-fix rule: never patch per-control what the engine got wrong.
- `(QUICK)` = under ~30 minutes.
- `Do it better` sub-lists are deliberate improvements over WinUI (kept separate from parity).
- Intentional deviations (eased reflow instead of snap+translate, springs for indicator motion)
  were excluded by the finders per `docs/guide/control-fidelity.md`.

## Headline items (user-reported, all confirmed with root cause)

1. **NavigationView child indentation**: ours `IndentStep = 24f` (`NavigationView.cs:815`) vs
   WinUI `c_itemIndentation = 31` px/level (`NavigationViewItemBase.h:63`). One-line fix.
2. **Hand cursor everywhere**: engine root cause — the reconciler defaults every `OnClick`
   element to `CursorId.Hand` (`src/FluentGpu.Reconciler/Reconciler.cs:1001`). WinUI's only
   control-level Hand is HyperlinkButton (+ inline text hyperlinks); everything else is arrow.
   Deleting the default heals **36 confirmed findings** across every clickable control. A second
   engine bug rides along: explicit `Arrow` can't mask an ancestor IBeam/Hand because Arrow
   doubles as the "unset" sentinel (`Columns.cs:265`, `InputDispatcher.cs:649`).
3. **PersonPicture "just plain wrong"**: the control's math is a faithful port (0.42 font
   fraction matches `PersonPicture.cpp:597`); the breakage is the engine's `ArrangeZStack`
   stretching unsized children and pinning them top-left, ignoring Justify
   (`PersonPicture.cs:103-110`, `FlexLayout.cs:578-585`) — initials are never centered. Compounded
   by Bold-700-vs-SemiBold-600 (no numeric FontWeight in TextEl) and a badge-clip bug currently
   masked because D3D12 `PushClip` is a no-op. API gaps: `ProfilePicture`, `Contact`,
   `BadgeText`, `BadgeImageSource`, `PreferSmallImage`.

## Scorecard

| Group | Areas | High | Med | Low |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| buttons-and-toggles | 4 | 6 | 20 | 32 |
| inputs | 7 | 15 | 64 | 69 |
| collections | 5 | 14 | 36 | 45 |
| navigation-chrome | 7 | 31 | 60 | 69 |
| surfaces-status-misc | 12 | 27 | 72 | 71 |
| engine-systemic | 5 | 43 | 23 | 35 |
| **Total** | **40** | **136** | **275** | **321** |

(38 of cursor-audit's 43 highs collapse into the single engine-01 fix. TabView (10 high),
FlipView/Swipe (7), DateTime (6), Pivot/SelectorBar and Panels (5 each) are the largest genuine
per-control debts.)

Per-area counts: see the per-control table at the end of this document.

## Execution waves

**Wave A — engine quick wins (≈1 day, erases ~50 findings incl. all three user reports)**
1. Delete the OnClick→Hand default (`Reconciler.cs:1001`); keep Hand opt-in (HyperlinkButton
   already sets it, EditableText already sets IBeam). Engine work item 1.
2. Explicit-cursor presence sentinel so Arrow terminates the cursor walk (TextBox delete button,
   PasswordBox eye, AutoSuggestBox query button). Engine work item 2.
3. `TextEl` default color `#E6E6E6` → `Tok.TextPrimary` (`Element.cs:303`) — wrong in both themes.
4. Light-theme elevation-gradient flip (tok-elev-flip-01) — affects every bordered control.
5. NavigationView `IndentStep` 24 → 31.
6. ToolTip wrapper: drop legacy `OnClick = Toggle` (makes any tooltipped element a Hand-cursored
   tab stop).
7. PersonPicture: wrap initials in a centering Box (not ZStack), remove root ClipToBounds,
   compute badge OffsetX explicitly (`size + 4 − plate`), badge `!= 0` rule.

**Wave B — input-semantics engine batch** (engine work items 3–12): Enter activates on key-UP
with pressed visual + `IsRepeat` guard for all clickables (incl. RepeatButton — WinUI repeats on
Space only); any-key-down cancels an armed press; AcceptsReturn/ActivateOnEnter opt-out; pressed
visual tracks pointer during hold; pointer focus on press (+ AllowFocusOnInteraction analogue);
pointer-cancel delivery to captured drag targets; middle-button routing (TabView middle-click
close); RepeatTicker per-node Delay/Interval + pointer-over pause; element-level wheel hook.

**Wave C — text pipeline** (engine work items 13–18): numeric FontWeight (SemiBold 600, SemiLight
350) + CharacterSpacing; LineHeight/LineStackingStrategy; TextLineBounds=Tight; inline-run model
(SpanTextEl) + hyperlink spans + read-only selection; per-control SelectionHighlightColor; type
ramp to WinUI values; Segoe UI Variable when the shaper is ready.

**Wave D — per-control parity batches** (high→medium, using the `winui-parity-batch` workflow):
order by debt and app relevance — TabView; DateTime (DatePicker/TimePicker/CalendarView);
FlipView/Swipe; Pivot/SelectorBar; BreadcrumbBar/PipsPager; CommandBarFlyout; SplitView;
ColorPicker; Panels; media chrome; then the medium tail per group. Collections + NavigationView
mediums fold in here too.

**Wave E — larger engine features, by need** (engine work items 19–44): BackgroundSizing inset
fill; absolute-extent gradient mapping (3px elevation band); measure-override seam (RelativePanel
graph, Viewbox, InfoBar orientation, RadioButtons columns); programmatic scroll controller + snap
points/fling; popup pass-through + FlyoutShowMode + 4px cascade overlap; focus system
(TabNavigation=Once, UseSystemFocusVisuals, last-input-device, per-element ring overrides);
AnimatedIcon keyframed-vector state machine; conic gradient (ColorPicker ring); ArcSpec override;
AnimEngine live-value retarget; RTL/FlowDirection sweep; KeyTips; PAL system params + sound seam;
TitleBar/drag regions + TabView tear-out windowing; media video surface; ParallaxView binding.

**Deferred / skip**: PullToRefresh, RichEditBox, InkCanvas/InkToolBar/MapControl, WebView2
hosting (engine work item 45).

## Verification

- `dotnet build` touched projects; headless deterministic checks in `src/FluentGpu.VerticalSlice`
  (reconcile/layout/anim assertions per `docs/guide/control-fidelity.md` §4).
- Screenshot gallery diffs: `FluentGpu.WindowsApp --screenshot out/x.png --shot <id> --frames N`
  for every touched control.
- Cursor sweep: hover every interactive control after Wave A — expect arrow everywhere except
  hyperlinks (Hand) and editable text (IBeam).
- Note: the PersonPicture badge-clip fix is invisible on D3D12 until `PushClip` is implemented —
  verify on the headless/golden path.

---

# Findings by group

## buttons-and-toggles

### button-family (Button, RepeatButton, HyperlinkButton, IconButton, ToggleButton)

- [high|bug] Held Enter auto-repeats clicks — ours: no `e.IsRepeat` guard on the Enter path (src/FluentGpu.Input/InputDispatcher.cs:724-728; Space has one at :736) vs WinUI: key-down ignored while `m_bIsSpaceOrEnterKeyDown` is set, so a held Enter yields exactly ONE click even on RepeatButton — only Space arms the 500/33 repeat timer (ButtonBaseKeyProcess.h:40; RepeatButton_Partial.cpp:212-217). Fix: ignore repeated Enter key-downs for ALL clickables, repeat nodes included. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Enter activates on key-DOWN with no pressed visual — ours: Enter invokes the click immediately on key-down, never sets `NodeFlags.Pressed` (InputDispatcher.cs:724-728; Button.cs:31 documents "Enter-down / Space-up") vs WinUI: KeyDown only sets `IsPressed=TRUE`, Click raised on KeyUp under `ClickMode_Release` (ButtonBaseKeyProcess.h:51, :110-113; ButtonBase_Partial.cpp:475-483 — deliberately moved to release for reentrancy). Fix: treat Enter like Space — Pressed on key-down, click on key-up. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Pressed visual doesn't track pointer during a hold — ours: `_pressed` set on down (InputDispatcher.cs:215), PointerMove (:150-195) only updates `_hovered`; pressed cleared solely on up/cancel (:273, :343) vs WinUI: `OnPointerMoved` sets `IsPressed = IsValidPointerPosition` (0.05px tolerance) — drag-off un-presses, drag-back re-presses while captured (ButtonBase_Partial.cpp:629-638, :602-606). Fix: re-evaluate Pressed on PointerMove while held — clear when pointer leaves `_down`'s bounds, restore on re-entry. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-api] SubtleButtonStyle variant missing — ours: only AccentStyle and StandardStyle (src/FluentGpu.Controls/Button.cs:99/:117) vs WinUI: `SubtleButtonStyle` with SubtleFillColorTransparent/Secondary/Tertiary bg, transparent disabled bg, TextFillColorPrimary/Secondary/Disabled fg (Button_themeresources.xaml:297-377, :17-28). Fix: add `Button.Subtle`: Background=Tok.FillSubtleTransparent, Hover=FillSubtleSecondary, Pressed=FillSubtleTertiary, DisabledBackground=FillSubtleTransparent, fg TextPrimary/TextPrimary/TextSecondary/TextDisabled. (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] Buttons stretch in cross-axis — ours: root sets no AlignSelf; BoxEl AlignSelf default Auto + parent AlignItems Stretch → full-width buttons in a column (Button.cs:151-182; src/FluentGpu.Dsl/Element.cs:217/:219) vs WinUI: `HorizontalAlignment=Left`, `VerticalAlignment=Center` (Button_themeresources.xaml:161-162; same in RepeatButton :85-86, ToggleButton :187-188, HyperlinkButton :58-59). Fix: set `AlignSelf=FlexAlign.Start` on button-family roots (or document the flex-stretch deviation as intentional). (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-api] RepeatButton Delay/Interval not settable per instance — ours: `InitialDelayMs=500`/`IntervalMs=33` are private consts (src/FluentGpu.Animation/RepeatTicker.cs:26-27); RepeatButton.cs Style (:30-60) exposes neither vs WinUI: `RepeatButton_Delay` default 500 / `RepeatButton_Interval` default 33 (DependencyProperty.cpp :705-725 window; RepeatButton_Partial.cpp:149-182 validation, :508-509/:556-563 timer consumption). Fix: add Delay/Interval to RepeatButton.Style; RepeatTicker.Arm reads the node's values instead of consts. (ENGINE)
- [medium|bug] Auto-repeat keeps firing after pointer drags off — ours: Tick has no pointer-over gate (RepeatTicker.cs:45-62); disarm only at InputDispatcher.cs:166-167/:271-272/:343-345; RepeatButton.cs:8-9 CLAIMS drag-off stops the timer — doc/impl mismatch vs WinUI: `UpdateRepeatState` requires `IsPointerOver`, tick stops when not over, re-enter restarts with a fresh Delay (RepeatButton_Partial.cpp:530-548, :565-574, :308-336). Fix: pause RepeatTicker when the pointer leaves the armed node's bounds while held; resume with fresh Delay on re-entry. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-behavior] Only Escape/Tab cancel a held Space press — ours: `_spaceArmed` cancels only at InputDispatcher.cs:708 (Escape), :702 (Tab), :918 (focus move) vs WinUI: ANY other key-down while Space/Enter held sets `IsPressed=FALSE` and clears the pending activation (ButtonBaseKeyProcess.h:64-70). Fix: cancel `_spaceArmed` (fire:false) on any other key-down while armed. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-behavior] Pointer focus moves on release, not press — ours: NearestFocusable focused inside PointerUp, only when released over the same node (InputDispatcher.cs:282-283) vs WinUI: `Focus(FocusState_Pointer)` + `CapturePointer` in OnPointerPressed (ButtonBase_Partial.cpp:700-709). Fix: move pointer-focus acquisition to the PointerDown edge. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-behavior] RepeatButton keyboard repeat rides OS auto-repeat, no pressed visual — ours: repeat nodes fire on every Space key-down incl. OS auto-repeat, never set Pressed (InputDispatcher.cs:731-734; self-documented RepeatButton.cs:13-15); Enter also repeats at OS rate (:724) vs WinUI: Space-down arms the same 500/33 timer (`m_keyboardCausingRepeat`), tick requires `IsPressed`, Enter yields a single click (RepeatButton_Partial.cpp:212-217, :567). Fix: arm RepeatTicker on first Space-down / disarm on key-up, set Pressed while held; per-instance Delay/Interval then applies to keyboard too once rb-01 lands. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-api] ClickMode (Release/Press/Hover) not exposed — ours: absent; hard-wired to release-activation (InputDispatcher.cs:274-284) vs WinUI: validation + Press→OnClick on pointer-down + Hover→OnClick on enter (ButtonBase_Partial.cpp:97-108, :713-716, :546-550); RepeatButton sets `ClickMode_Press` at Initialize (RepeatButton_Partial.cpp:29). Fix: expose press/hover activation modes, or document release-only as supported. (ENGINE)
- [low|engine-gap] `BackgroundSizing=InnerBorderEdge` rendered as OuterBorderEdge — ours: every fill drawn to the outer rounded-rect edge; documented E9 gap (Button.cs:11-14) vs WinUI: DefaultButtonStyle InnerBorderEdge vs Accent OuterBorderEdge (Button_themeresources.xaml:156/:238); ToggleButton flips per checked state (ToggleButton_themeresources.xaml:255-257/271-273/287-289). Fix: E9 primitive — inset fill rect/radii by BorderWidth when InnerBorderEdge. (ENGINE)
- [low|styling-delta] HyperlinkButton 2px smaller than WinUI — ours: no BorderWidth set; comment :116-118 overclaims pixel-identity (src/FluentGpu.Controls/HyperlinkButton.cs:106-118) vs WinUI: `HyperlinkButtonBorderThemeThickness=1` occupies layout, +1px per side around Padding 11,5,11,6 (HyperlinkButton_themeresources.xaml:17, :56). Fix: Padding 12,6,12,7 — note BorderWidth is paint-only in this engine (FlexLayout has no border term; paint column src/FluentGpu.Scene/Columns.cs:101), so the transparent-border alternative would NOT fix layout. (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] IconButton scales every glyph on hover/press — ours: `IconHoverScale=1.08`/`IconPressScale=0.88` applied to the wrapper for ALL glyphs (src/FluentGpu.Controls/IconButton.cs:45-46, :72) vs WinUI: states swap colors only; `AnimatedIcon.State` animates only AnimatedIcon content, static FontIcon glyphs never move (Button_themeresources.xaml:192/:208). Fix: default both scales to 1.0; keep scale as opt-in for AnimatedIcon-style glyphs. (QUICK)
- [low|missing-behavior] IconButton takes focus on click — ours: `Focusable=true` (IconButton.cs:96) + engine focuses NearestFocusable on release (InputDispatcher.cs:282-283) vs WinUI: AppBarButton sets `AllowFocusOnInteraction=False` (AppBarButton_themeresources.xaml:136). Fix: add an AllowFocusOnInteraction analogue (skip pointer-focus, keep tab-focus); set it on IconButton. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-api] Button.Flyout association missing — ours: factories take only onClick (Button.cs:136-139; DropDownButton.cs is the dedicated flyout button) vs WinUI: OnClick auto-opens the associated Flyout via `ShowAt(this)` + routes its accelerators (Button_Partial.cpp:85-87, :136-155, :157-169). Fix: document composition (onClick → OverlayHost.Open(anchor,…)) or add an optional flyout-builder param opening after Click. (QUICK)

Do it better:
- [low|improvement] Per-instance underline opt-in beats WinUI's app-global `HyperlinkUnderlineVisible` resource (HyperlinkButton.cs:50-55 vs Hyperlink_themeresources.xaml:20, HyperLinkButton_Partial.cpp:207-212). Keep; ensure the E8 HighContrast structural override stays non-suppressible.
- [low|improvement] Explicit `CheckState` + onCycle avoids WinUI's nullable `IsChecked` footgun (ToggleButton.cs:106-115 vs ToggleButton_Partial.cpp:249-301). Keep — cycle parity with OnToggleImpl verified.

*Intentional deviations (keep documented, don't "fix"): 83ms BrushTransition over-coverage on border brushes (Button.cs:85-89, ToggleButton.cs:37-41); eased foreground ramps vs WinUI's discrete KeyTime=0 swaps (ToggleButton.cs:143-144). Token/metric matrices (Padding 11,5,11,6; CornerRadius 4; Border 1; FontSize 14; FocusVisualMargin -3; full ToggleButton 3×4 state matrix) verified exact.*

### split-dropdown (DropDownButton, SplitButton, ToggleSplitButton)

- [high|bug] Hand cursor on all three controls; WinUI uses Arrow — ours: no Cursor set in DropDownButton.cs (:152), SplitButton.cs (:156/:181), ToggleSplitButton.cs (:166/:180); engine defaults OnClick nodes to Hand (Reconciler.cs:998-1001) vs WinUI: no SetCursor in SplitButton.cpp/DropDownButton.cpp — arrow everywhere (our Button.cs:176-178 documents the convention). Fix: `Cursor = CursorId.Arrow` on DropDownButton root, both SplitButton halves + root, both ToggleSplitButton halves + root. (QUICK)
- [high|bug] Halves become extra tab stops (3 stops vs WinUI's 1) — ours: halves have OnClick but no `TabStop=false` (SplitButton.cs:144-160, :171-200; ToggleSplitButton.cs:160-168, :174-196); Reconciler.cs:1111 auto-derives focusable from OnClick vs WinUI: inner buttons `IsTabStop="False"`, control itself IsTabStop=True (SplitButton.xaml:227-228, :15). Fix: `TabStop = false` on primary/secondary half BoxEls in both controls (pattern: EditableText.cs:450, ScrollBar.cs:437). (QUICK)
- [high|bug] ToggleSplitButton: Enter/Space on the focused root do not toggle — ours: root has no OnClick, OnKeyDown handles only Keys.Down (ToggleSplitButton.cs:214); engine activation requires ClickBit on the focused node (InputDispatcher.cs:719-726); doc :22-23 claims it works vs WinUI: Space/Enter key-up → OnClickPrimary → Toggle() (SplitButton.cpp:334-349; ToggleSplitButton.cpp:53-58). Fix: handle Keys.Enter/Keys.Space in root OnKeyDown → `Flip()` + `e.Handled=true` (mirror SplitButton.cs:103-107). (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] ToggleSplitButton missing F4 open chord; stale deferral comment — ours: opens only on Keys.Down (ToggleSplitButton.cs:214); comment :212-213 claims KeyEventArgs lacks modifiers, but `KeyEventArgs.Mods` exists (Events.cs:26) and SplitButton.cs:108 already handles F4 vs WinUI: F4 opens (SplitButton.cpp:362-367), Alt+Down opens (:350-360). Fix: add Keys.F4 to the open chord; delete the stale comment. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] SplitButton Enter/Space invoke on key-DOWN with auto-repeat — ours: OnKey calls OnInvoke with no `e.IsRepeat` guard (SplitButton.cs:100-107) vs WinUI: KeyDown only sets `m_isKeyDown` visual; OnClickPrimary fires once in OnSplitButtonKeyUp (SplitButton.cpp:324-349). Fix: minimum `!e.IsRepeat` guard; ideally fire on key-up with pressed visual while held. (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] Disabled SplitButton hides the 1px divider — ours: `Fill = enabled ? Tok.StrokeControlDefault : ColorF.Transparent` (SplitButton.cs:166); ToggleSplitButton.cs:135 keeps it visible when disabled — internally inconsistent vs WinUI: Disabled state never touches DividerBackgroundGrid — stays SplitButtonBorderBrushDivider = ControlStrokeColorDefaultBrush (SplitButton.xaml:71-79, :225; _themeresources:27). Fix: divider `Fill = Tok.StrokeControlDefault` regardless of enabled. (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] DropDownButton stretches in a stretch container — ours: root BoxEl has no AlignSelf (DropDownButton.cs:127-156; SplitButton.cs:212 and ToggleSplitButton.cs:203 both already set FlexAlign.Start) vs WinUI: `HorizontalAlignment=Left` (DropDownButton.xaml:9). Fix: `AlignSelf = FlexAlign.Start` on the DropDownButton root. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-api] Flyout limited to MenuFlyoutItem lists with hardcoded placement — ours: `IReadOnlyList<MenuFlyoutItem> Items` (SplitButton.cs:53, ToggleSplitButton.cs:36, DropDownButton.cs:42); placement fixed to FlyoutPlacement.BottomLeft (SplitButton.cs:84) vs WinUI: `FlyoutBase Flyout { get; set; }` — any content; DropDownButton uses the flyout's own Placement (SplitButton.idl:20; DropDownButton.cpp:48). Fix: optional `Func<Element>? FlyoutContent` + placement override alongside Items, via the same OverlayHost path.
- [low|missing-behavior] SplitButton opens flyout on plain Down; WinUI requires Alt+Down — ours: `Keys.Down || Keys.F4` → ToggleMenu, no Alt check (SplitButton.cs:108-112; ToggleSplitButton.cs:214 same) vs WinUI: Down opens only with Alt key state Down (SplitButton.cpp:350-360). Fix: gate Down on `(e.Mods & KeyModifiers.Alt) != 0`, keep F4 unguarded. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] ToggleSplitButton checked+disabled renders accent-dim + transparent border — ours: disabled+checked → Tok.AccentDisabled fill, transparent border (ToggleSplitButton.cs:95, :129) vs WinUI: `!IsEnabled` always goes to "Disabled" — SplitButtonBorderBrushDisabled (StrokeControlDefault) + gray SplitButtonBackgroundDisabled; CheckedDisabled tokens (_themeresources:12,31) never referenced by the template (SplitButton.cpp:133-135; SplitButton.xaml:71-79). Fix: render unchecked disabled chrome (FillControlDisabled + StrokeControlDefault) when disabled, or record ours as an intentional token-intent deviation.
- [low|styling-delta] Focus ring margin -3 vs WinUI -1 — ours: neither file sets FocusVisualMargin; engine default Edges4.All(-3) (Reconciler.cs:1113) vs WinUI: SplitButton.xaml:14 `FocusVisualMargin="-1"` (DropDownButton.xaml:15 is -3, so DropDownButton matches). Fix: `FocusVisualMargin = Edges4.All(-1)` on SplitButton/ToggleSplitButton roots. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Pressed half should flatten its outer border to solid StrokeControlDefault — ours: root border static per render (elevation gradient at rest); halves have no borders (SplitButton.cs:216-218) vs WinUI: PrimaryPressed/SecondaryPressed → per-half BorderBrush = SplitButtonBorderBrushPressed = StrokeControlDefault (SplitButton.xaml:112, :128; _themeresources:25). Fix: per-half overlay border (radii 4,0,0,4 / 0,4,4,0) with PressedBorderBrush = solid StrokeControlDefault, or accept the 1px-bottom-edge delta.
- [low|missing-behavior] No keyboard-held / touch pressed visual — ours: no key-held pressed visual, no pointer-device-type branch in either file vs WinUI: `m_isKeyDown` → SecondaryButtonSpan; touch/key-held → TouchPressed/CheckedTouchPressed (both halves pressed at once) (SplitButton.cpp:121-128, :152-156/:186-195). Fix: while Space/Enter held or on touch press, set both halves' fill to the pressed token. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-api] DropDownButton has no arbitrary-content slot — ours: only Label + Glyph (DropDownButton.cs:40-41; SplitButton.cs:51 already has `Element? PrimaryContent`) vs WinUI: derives from Button (ContentControl), ContentPresenter at DropDownButton.xaml:92. Fix: add `Element? Content` mirroring SplitButton.PrimaryContent, mounted in the star column before the chevron. (QUICK)
- [low|bug] ToggleSplitButton root PressedBorderBrush is dead code — ours: set at ToggleSplitButton.cs:206 but root has no OnClick/OnPointerDown so it never enters pressed; :125-129 menuOpen/checked branches already cover visible cases. Fix: remove it (or move pressed-border handling to the halves per style-05). (QUICK)
- [low|bug] ToggleSplitButton `Flip()` uses render-time captured `on` — ours: `bool next = !on;` with `on` captured at :62 (ToggleSplitButton.cs:87) — stale on external IsChecked change vs WinUI: Toggle() reads live `IsChecked(!IsChecked())` (ToggleSplitButton.cpp:65-68). Fix: `bool next = !IsChecked.Value;` inside Flip. (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] Chevron is static; WinUI AnimatedChevronDownSmall plays hover/press micro-animation — ours: static TextEl color ramp only (DropDownButton.cs:117-121, SplitButton.cs:189-194, ToggleSplitButton.cs:188-192) — this is WinUI's FontIcon fallback path vs WinUI: `AnimatedIcon.State = PointerOver/Pressed` on the 12x12 AnimatedChevronDownSmallVisualSource (DropDownButton.xaml:44/:63/:93-98; SplitButton.xaml:44-51/:230-235). Fix: AnimatedIcon-style keyframe vector support; fallback is a legitimate WinUI path, low priority. (ENGINE)

Do it better:
- [low|improvement] DropDownButton's Down/F4 open chords don't exist in WinUI (DropDownButton.cpp has no key handling; only Button click opens, Button_Partial.cpp:85-86) — keep as a keyboard-discoverability improvement, but fix the DropDownButton.cs:153 comment claiming WinUI parity; consider gating Down on Alt for consistency.

*Intentional deviations: chevron does NOT rotate on open — this MATCHES WinUI (no Expanded state; DropDownButton.cs:20-21); hover/press easing Easing.FluentPopOpen cubic(0,0,0,1) @83ms = documented equivalent of ControlFastOutSlowInKeySpline + BrushTransition 0:0:0.083. Glyph E96E @ FontSize 8 in 12x12 box Margin 8,0,0,0, 35/35 columns, 1px separator, padding 11,6,11,7, full token matrix incl. ControlStrokeColorOnAccentTertiary #37000000 — all verified exact.*

### checkbox-radio (CheckBox, RadioButton, RadioButtons)

- [high|bug] Hand cursor over CheckBox/RadioButton — ours: OnClick set but never Cursor (CheckBox.cs:146-166, RadioButton.cs:196-215); Reconciler.cs:1001 defaults clickables to Hand vs WinUI: arrow over toggles, hand only on hyperlinks (templates define no cursor — CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:297-298, RadioButton_themeresources.xaml:200-201). Fix: `Cursor = CursorId.Arrow` on root BoxEl in CheckBox.Build and RadioButton.Build (Group/RadioButtons inherit). (QUICK)
- [medium|bug] Checkmark/dash props frozen after mount — stale glyph color on disable — ours: Size/Color/Pressable passed via Embed.Comp factory closure (CheckBox.cs:107-109); Reconciler.cs:215-221 reuses same-type ComponentEl WITHOUT re-running the factory, so a checked box that gets disabled keeps TextOnAccentPrimary vs WinUI: CheckedDisabled glyph → TextOnAccentFillColorDisabledBrush, IndeterminateDisabled same (CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:72, :76). Fix: flow glyph props through a Context provider (RadioButtons.Props pattern, RadioButtons.cs:52-58) or key the mark by (state,enabled).
- [medium|missing-behavior] Enter toggles CheckBox/RadioButton; WinUI ignores Enter — ours: InputDispatcher.cs:724-728 fires OnClick on Enter for every clickable vs WinUI: `SetAcceptsReturn(false)` on both — only Space (key-up) toggles (CheckBox_Partial.cpp:27, RadioButton_Partial.cpp:30). Fix: add `BoxEl.AcceptsReturn` (default true) honored at InputDispatcher.cs:724; set false on CheckBox/RadioButton roots. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Standalone RadioButton/Group: no arrow-key focus roving with wrap — ours: `onKeyDown:null` (RadioButton.cs:99-100); Group self-documents "every item is a tab stop, no arrow roving" (:233-234) vs WinUI: Down/Right→next, Up/Left→prev radio (keyboard OriginalKey only), wrap last→first (RadioButton_Partial.cpp:583-595, :631-639); focus moves WITHOUT selecting. Fix: wire arrow roving ±1 with wrap, focus-only — but KEEP items as individual tab stops (WinUI standalone radios each remain tab stops; roving navigates via GetNextTabStop/GetPreviousTabStop :633/:638; single-tab-stop is only the RadioButtons container contract, RadioButtons.xaml:5-6).
- [medium|missing-behavior] RadioButtons MaxColumns not clamped by available width — ours: `cols = min(MaxColumns, n)` only (RadioButtons.cs:78; doc :13-14 admits the gap) vs WinUI: effective columns = `min(requested, floor((availableWidth-maxItemWidth)/(ColumnSpacing+maxItemWidth))+1)`, min 1 (ColumnMajorUniformToLargestGridLayout.cpp:145-162). Fix: width-aware column count — needs a measure-time custom-layout hook. (ENGINE)
- [medium|styling-delta] RadioButtons grid not uniform-to-largest — ours: independent vertical stacks with Gap, each item natural-sized (RadioButtons.cs:151-166) vs WinUI: MeasureOverride sizes EVERY cell to the largest child's width/height — equal columns, aligned rows (ColumnMajorUniformToLargestGridLayout.cpp:16-43). Fix: compute largest item size and force uniform cell Width/Height = max.
- [low|missing-behavior] Pressed checkmark/dash doesn't dim — ours: `GlyphFg.Resting(enabled)` only; the Pressed leg (CheckBox.cs:70) is dead; PolylineStrokeEl has no Hover/PressedColor (Element.cs:254-291, only Color at :263) vs WinUI: CheckBoxCheckGlyphForegroundCheckedPressed → TextOnAccentFillColorSecondaryBrush; IndeterminatePressed same (CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:71, :75). Fix: add PressedColor to PolylineStrokeEl (eased like TextEl.PressedColor, Element.cs:308-309), pass GlyphFg.Pressed. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-behavior] CheckBox missing numpad +/- keys — ours: no OnKeyDown in CheckBox.cs vs WinUI: when `!IsThreeState && IsEnabled`, VirtualKey_Add → IsChecked=true, Subtract → false (CheckBox_Partial.cpp:48-68). Fix: OnKeyDown on root — Add→onChange(Checked), Subtract→onChange(Unchecked), two-state only, Handled=true. (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] Uncheck removes the checkmark instantly; WinUI plays a ~67.5ms un-draw — ours: unchecked mounts no child (CheckBox.cs:106-110); the mark carries no transition spec. Note: the engine HAS an exit path (Reconciler.cs:842-848 orphans + AnimEngine.SeedExit, AnimEngine.cs:385-393) but it drives only Opacity/Translate/Scale — no StrokeTrimEnd channel, and PolylineStrokeEl/ComponentEl can't carry an Animate spec vs WinUI: NormalOnToNormalOff 0.0→0.0253125 of 26666666 ticks ≈ 67.5ms; PointerOverOn/PressedOn ≈ 66.7ms (AnimatedAcceptVisualSource.cpp:1945-1946, :105, :1957, :1969). Fix: TrimEnd 1→0 over 67.5ms before unmount — needs a keyframe-channel exit hook. (ENGINE)
- [low|motion-delta] Indeterminate dash draws on over 200ms; WinUI hard-cuts — ours: DrawnDash plays a 200ms StrokeTrimEnd reveal (CheckBox.cs:238, :243-244); 200f is not a WinUI token vs WinUI: Normal/PointerOver/PressedIndeterminate are position-only markers — AnimatedIcon cuts to the frame; fallback FontIcon E9AE 12px (AnimatedAcceptVisualSource.cpp:1981-1983; CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:277, :607). Fix: snap the dash in (duration 0) for 1:1, or keep and self-document as improvement. (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] Unchecked-pressed proto-dot fades in over 167ms; WinUI shows it instantly — ours: Opacity 0 → PressedOpacity 1 rides the eased press progress (PressDurationMs 167) (RadioButton.cs:159-163; Element.cs:133, :144-152) vs WinUI: PressedCheckGlyph Opacity KeyTime 0 Value 1; only Width/Height animate 4→10 over 167ms (RadioButton_themeresources.xaml:298-306). Fix: make PressedOpacity step at press start (or an OpacityStep flag) while scale animates. (ENGINE)
- [low|styling-delta] Glyph vs label vertical alignment differs for wrapped/multiline content — ours: single rows, AlignItems=Center + Gap; top padding 5/6 dropped (CheckBox.cs:146-152, RadioButton.cs:196-201) vs WinUI: CheckBox box VerticalAlignment=Center, label VerticalContentAlignment=Top + Padding 8,5,0,0 + TextWrapping=Wrap (CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:602, :274, :287, :611); RadioButton glyph grid Top Height=32, Padding 8,6,0,0 (:370, :187). - [low|styling-delta] CheckGlyph 1px vertical nudge (checked) missing — ours: mark centered, no offset (CheckBox.cs:115-128) vs WinUI: CheckGlyph `Margin="0,1,0,-1"` when checked; indeterminate resets to 0 (CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:604, :505/:534/:563). - [low|missing-api] String-only content/header APIs — CheckBox.Create takes string label only (CheckBox.cs:74-79); RadioButton's Element content seam is internal (RadioButton.cs:102-110), public Create string-only (:97-100); RadioButtons header string-only, no SelectedItem/HeaderTemplate-shaped API (RadioButtons.cs:34-50) vs WinUI: both ContentControls with arbitrary Content (CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:611; RadioButton_themeresources.xaml:378); RadioButtons.idl:20-28 SelectedIndex AND SelectedItem + SelectionChanged, Header Object + HeaderTemplate, ContainerFromIndex (:17). Fix: public `Create(Element content, ...)` overloads on both + Element header overload on RadioButtons; index→item is caller-derivable.

### toggleswitch

- [high|styling-delta] Hand cursor over ToggleSwitch — ours: no Cursor set anywhere in src/FluentGpu.Controls/ToggleSwitch.cs; root row has OnClick (:359), Reconciler.cs:1000-1001 defaults to Hand vs WinUI: template (ToggleSwitch_themeresources.xaml:190-536) sets no cursor — system arrow (convention: Button.cs:178). Fix: `Cursor = CursorId.Arrow` on the root BoxEl (~:348) and re-assert in the PartRoot Parts.Apply block (:369-378). (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] No default On/Off content labels — ours: onContent/offContent default null (ToggleSwitch.cs:124-126); label only rendered when non-empty (:342-345) vs WinUI: OnContent/OffContent default to localized TEXT_TOGGLESWITCH_ON/OFF ("On"/"Off") (ToggleSwitch_Partial.cpp:308-329). Fix: default `onContent="On"`, `offContent="Off"` in Create (localizable), explicit empty string opts out. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Enter toggles the switch; WinUI ignores Enter — ours: InputDispatcher.cs:724-727 fires click on Enter key-down BEFORE OnKeyDown routing (:746-751); root OnClick (:359) toggles, no opt-out vs WinUI: HandlesKey = Space/GamepadA only; Enter never handled (ToggleSwitch_Partial.cpp:1002-1007; KeyUp gate ToggleSwitchKeyProcess.h:35-48). Fix: per-node flag (e.g. `ActivateOnEnter=false`) or route OnKeyDown before Enter activation. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Drag-to-toggle cancels when pointer exits bounds — ours: `Exit()` sets g.Cancelled + Reset(), the outside release is consumed silently (ToggleSwitch.cs:217-225, :199-204) vs WinUI: Thumb keeps capture — DragCompletedHandler → MoveCompleted half-crossing toggle fires wherever release happens (ToggleSwitch_Partial.cpp:844-866, :592-617; OnPointerCaptureLost :733-746 only clears pointer-over). Fix: control-side only — the engine already routes OnDrag with no bounds check (InputDispatcher.cs:185-188) and delivers the outside release via implicit capture (:287-301); make `Exit()` cancel only un-moved presses (`g.Moved == false`, tap path) and keep the gesture alive when moved so Release() applies the existing half-crossing rule (ToggleSwitch.cs:207-211). (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] Click target + focus ring span the 154px MinWidth row — ours: OnClick, Focusable, FocusVisualMargin(-7,-3) all on the row BoxEl with MinWidth=154/MinHeight=40 — empty space right of the label toggles; ring ≥154+14 × 40+6 (ToggleSwitch.cs:348-365) vs WinUI: tap surface = SwitchThumb spanning the inner Auto+12+Auto grid at FULL 40px height (RowSpan=3/ColumnSpan=3, template:524, inner grid HorizontalAlignment=Left :493); focus target = SwitchAreaGrid Margin 0,5 with IsTemplateFocusTarget (template:504) → ring ≈ (40+12+content)+14 × 30+6; MinWidth 154 only pads layout. Fix: inner box wrapping track+gap+label at FULL row height carries OnClick/Focusable (no 5px inset on the tap surface — that would make it 30px vs WinUI's 40px); get the 30+6-tall ring via `FocusVisualMargin (-7, 2, -7, 2)` on that box (or a separate non-interactive focus box); keep MinWidth=154 on a non-interactive outer box.
- [low|missing-api] Header/OnContent/OffContent string-only — ours: Props carry `string?`; PartContentLabel/PartHeader are TextEl-only parts (ToggleSwitch.cs:118-119, :124-126, :50-54) vs WinUI: Header/HeaderTemplate, OffContent/OffContentTemplate, OnContent/OnContentTemplate are IInspectable + DataTemplate (ToggleSwitch_Partial.cpp:374-404; template:492/:505-506). Fix: Element overloads for header/onContent/offContent (or document `Parts.Set<TextEl>` as the styling-only escape hatch).

Do it better:
- [low|improvement] Directional Arrow/Home/End toggles are dead code in shipped WinUI 3 — ours implements the intent (ToggleSwitch.cs:235-245: Left/Down/Home→off, Right/Up/End→on; comment :237 wrongly cites ToggleSwitchKeyProcess.h:52-71 as parity). WinUI gates the directional block on handlesKey but HandlesKey = Space/GamepadA only, so arrows never toggle (ToggleSwitchKeyProcess.h:48; ToggleSwitch_Partial.cpp:1005-1006, :776). Keep the behavior; correct the doc comment; swap Left/Right under RTL when the engine grows FlowDirection.

*Intentional deviations (all self-documented): knob travel Motion.ControlFast 167ms + FluentPopOpen for WinUI's OS-PVL RepositionThemeAnimation; knob rest x=4 vs WinUI 3.5 (0.5px rounding); single-rect 83ms brush cross-fade vs two-rect opacity cross-fade; key-down vs key-up timing; 4px Win32 drag-box threshold. Core fidelity verified exact: track 40x20 r10, knob 12/14/17x14 pinned 3px, travel 20, 83ms + (0,0,0,1), 250ms disabled return, MinWidth 154, half-crossing rule. Engine-wide gap not filed per-control: WinUI plays ElementSound Invoke on toggle (cpp:520).*

**Effort:** button-family **M** (8 ENGINE items in InputDispatcher/RepeatTicker/E9, each small but cross-cutting; styles are quick) · split-dropdown **S** (almost all QUICK control-side fixes; only behavior-01/motion-01 are ENGINE and deferrable) · checkbox-radio **M** (context plumbing, uniform-to-largest grid, AcceptsReturn/PressedColor/exit-keyframe engine hooks) · toggleswitch **S** (one ENGINE flag; rest are quick control-side edits).
Suggested order: split-dropdown + toggleswitch quick wins first (cursor/tab/key fixes are user-visible bugs), then the shared InputDispatcher Enter/Space/pressed-tracking batch (fixes bb-01/02/03/05, cb-enter-toggle, ts-key-enter-01 together), then checkbox-radio layout/motion work.

Fix: clear updatingText inside OnTextChanged (consume-once flag) or compare against the last self-written string.

**Do it better**
- [low|improvement] Expression evaluator beats WinUI's: unary minus before parens and right-associative '^' — ours: unary-minus token 'u' (NumberBox.cs:566-571); '^' right-assoc → "2^3^2"=512, "-(2+3)"=-5 (:636-637) vs WinUI: regex `^-?([^-+/*\(\)\^\s]+)` can't match '-(' → "-(2+3)" errors; '^' left-assoc → "2^3^2"=64 (NumberBoxParser.cpp:74-93, :124-137). - [low|styling-delta] Missing FocusVisualMargin -8,-7,-8,0 (QUICK) — ours: root BoxEl (RatingControl.cs:393-403) sets Focusable only; BoxEl supports it (Element.cs:121) vs WinUI: `<Setter Property="FocusVisualMargin" Value="-8,-7,-8,0" />` (RatingControl.xaml:15). Fix: FocusVisualMargin = new Edges4(-8,-7,-8,0) on the root.
- [low|motion-delta] Touch press lifts scale scalar to 1.0; WinUI's c_touchOverScale is dead code (always 0.8) (QUICK) — ours: PressInfo sets pointerScalar to TouchOverScale=1.0 on touch (cell scale 2.0 = 32px) (RatingControl.cs:239-246) vs WinUI: c_touchOverScale=1.0 defined (cpp:20) but pointerScalar written exactly once with c_mouseOverScale (cpp:116) — always 0.8. Fix: drop the touch switch (always MouseOverScale) for exact parity, or keep and re-document as intentional improvement (in-code comments currently mis-attribute it to WinUI).
- [low|missing-behavior] Value coercion is render-only; WinUI writes coerced value back — ours: Coerce() at render; signal keeps raw value (0.5 or 7 with max 5 read back unchanged) (RatingControl.cs:211-212, 457-469) vs WinUI: OnPropertyChanged SetValue()s the coerced value back (cpp:624-634); lowering MaxRating writes Value/PlaceholderValue down (cpp:602-622). Fix: write coerced value back into the Value signal; clamp Value/PlaceholderValue when MaxRating shrinks.
- [low|bug] Sweep dedupe compares against stale render snapshot — can miss a setPreview — ours: previewRef updated then `if (v != preview) setPreview(v)` against the render-time snapshot; two moves in one frame (3 then back to 2 when rendered preview==2) skip the second setPreview (RatingControl.cs:233-234) vs WinUI: every PointerMoved recomputes m_mousePercentage and unconditionally calls UpdateRatingItemsAppearance() (cpp:807-822). Fix: drop the `!= preview` guard (UseState setter de-dupes against pending) or gate on a lastDispatched ref.
- [low|missing-behavior] No RTL keyboard reversal (ENGINE) — ours: fixed map Left/Down=-1, Right/Up=+1 (RatingControl.cs:277-287) vs WinUI: flowDirectionReverser=-1 under RightToLeft flips Left/Right; Up/Down unflipped (cpp:955-973). Fix: when an RTL/FlowDirection seam lands, multiply the Left/Right delta by -1 in RTL.
- [low|missing-behavior] Gamepad focus-engagement model missing (A commits, B reverts) (ENGINE) — ours: no engagement/preEngagement state; engine already translates gamepad keys (InputDispatcher.cs:660-668: GamepadA→Enter, GamepadB→Escape, DPad/left-thumbstick→XY focus; Events.cs:116-119) — so today DPad on a focused rating moves focus away and GamepadA routes to a no-op click; divergence is concrete now vs WinUI: IsFocusEngagementEnabled=True (RatingControl.xaml:16); OnPreviewKeyDown GamepadA commits / GamepadB restores m_preEngagementValue firing ValueChanged, Enter/ExitGamepadEngagementMode with Invoke/GoBack sounds (cpp:1025-1140). Fix: add a focus-engagement seam, then preEngagementValue capture + A/B commit/revert.
- [low|engine-gap] ElementSound cues not played (Invoke on commit, Focus on dpad) (ENGINE) — ours: self-documented pending the IPlatformSound PAL seam (RatingControl.cs:261) vs WinUI: ElementSoundPlayer::Play(Invoke) on release (cpp:898); Focus sound for dpad/thumbstick (cpp:976-980). Fix: wire once IPlatformSound exists.
- [low|bug] Gallery shows "-1 / 5" after clearing (QUICK) — ours: src/FluentGpu.WindowsApp/ControlGalleryPages.cs:438 LiveText `$"{(int)val.Value} / 5"` prints the -1 sentinel vs WinUI: Value default -1 = "no value", never user-facing (RatingControl.idl:69-73). Fix: `val.Value <= 0 ? "unset" : $"{(int)val.Value} / 5"`.

**Do it better**
- [low|improvement] Dim unset outline stars when disabled (WinUI never finished its disabled state) — ours: StateBg = Tok.TextSecondary unconditionally, faithfully mirroring WinUI (RatingControl.cs:43,100) vs WinUI: "TODO: MSFT 11521414 - complete disabled state functionality" (cpp:265,307-312); Disabled state only retargets ForegroundContentPresenter (RatingControl.xaml:23-27). Optionally map bg → Tok.TextDisabled when !IsEnabled; if done, mark as intentional deviation in the doc comment.

### ColorPicker

- [high|missing-behavior] Default spectrum axes + third-dimension slider wrong (S/V box + hue rail vs WinUI Hue/Sat box + Value slider) — ours: spectrum maps x=saturation, y=value (src/FluentGpu.Controls/ColorPicker.cs:127-148); rail is a rainbow hue gradient (:160-181) vs WinUI: default Components=HueSaturation (ColorPicker.idl:45-46); box x=hue, y=saturation (ColorSpectrum.cpp:652-655); third-dimension channel=Value (ColorPicker.cpp:1162-1165), gradient black→color at current hue/sat (:1096-1097). - [high|bug] One-way binding: external writes to the Color signal after mount ignored — ours: seeds h/sat/val/alpha from Color.Peek() once (ColorPicker.cs:94-98); no effect re-syncs vs WinUI: OnColorChanged recomputes m_currentHsv + UpdateColorControls on every external set (ColorPicker.cpp:310-324). - [medium|bug] Hovering today replaces the accent disc with subtle gray (QUICK) — ours: today Fill=AccentDefault but HoverFill=Tok.FillSubtleSecondary / PressedFill=FillSubtleTertiary apply to ALL cells (CalendarView.cs:81-85) vs WinUI: TodayHoverBackground=AccentFillColorSecondary, TodayPressedBackground=AccentFillColorTertiary (CalendarView_themeresources.xaml:49-50). - [medium|styling-delta] Weekday header hardcoded English 'Mo..Su', Monday-first, 14px Bold — ours: static ["Mo".."Su"] (CalendarView.cs:19); Monday-first hardcoded (:59); TextEl Size 14 Bold (:51) vs WinUI: WeekDayNameStyle = CaptionTextBlockStyle (12px) + CalendarViewWeekDayFontWeight SemiBold (CalendarView_themeresources.xaml:325-331, :80), localized via DayOfWeekFormat/TemplateSettings (:713-719); FirstDayOfWeek from culture (CalendarView_Partial.cpp:261-262). Fix: localize abbreviations from CultureInfo, first day from culture (Sunday in en-US), 12px SemiBold TextPrimary.
- [low|styling-delta] Root missing its own chrome (bg/border/radius) — ours: root BoxEl no Fill/Border (CalendarView.cs:111-118); gallery wraps manually (DateTimePages.cs:15) vs WinUI: Background=ControlFillColorInputActive, BorderBrush=ControlStrokeColorDefault (CalendarView_themeresources.xaml:20-21); BorderThickness 1, CornerRadius ControlCornerRadius (:312,319,323); header divider = BorderBrush 1px (:685). Fix: ControlFillInputActive fill, 1px StrokeControlDefault border, 4px corners; divider uses border brush.
- [low|missing-api] Density bars and blackout strikethrough missing — ours: absent vs WinUI: CalendarViewDayItem.SetDensityColors; CalendarViewBlackoutStrikethroughBrush=ControlStrongStrokeColorDefault (CalendarView_themeresources.xaml:33). Fix: per-day density color bars at cell bottom; blackout days strikethrough + non-interactive.
- [low|styling-delta] Day cells lack the 1px margin (2px gutters both axes) (QUICK) — ours: 40x40 cells packed flush horizontally; rows Gap=2 vertical only (CalendarView.cs:75-79, :109) vs WinUI: CalendarViewDayItem Margin=1, MinWidth/MinHeight 40 (CalendarView_themeresources.xaml:246, :244-245). Fix: 1px margin around each 40px cell.

### CalendarDatePicker

- [high|missing-behavior] Selection never wired back; flyout never closes on pick — ours: doc admits 'selection isn't wired back' (CalendarDatePicker.cs:12-13); opens CalendarView.Create() with no callback (:29) — DateText never updates, flyout stays open vs WinUI: subscribes CalendarView SelectedDatesChanged (CalendarDatePicker_Partial.cpp:201-204); closes (IsCalendarOpen=FALSE), sets Date, fires DateChanged (:269). Fix: pass an OnSelectedDate callback into CalendarView; on pick set the date signal, close the overlay, fire OnDateChanged.
- [medium|missing-api] Missing public props/events — ours: Create() parameterless (CalendarDatePicker.cs:17); date internal UseState (:21) vs WinUI: forwards MinDate/MaxDate/IsTodayHighlighted/DisplayMode/FirstDayOfWeek/DayOfWeekFormat/CalendarIdentifier to the CalendarView (CalendarDatePicker_themeresources.xaml:203); PlaceholderText default localized (Partial.cpp:46-48); DateChanged/Opened/Closed events. Fix: Signal<DateOnly?> Date, PlaceholderText, Header, MinDate/MaxDate + passthroughs, OnDateChanged.
- [low|styling-delta] Date format hardcoded 'MMM d, yyyy'; WinUI default culture ShortDate (QUICK) — ours: d.ToString("MMM d, yyyy") (CalendarDatePicker.cs:52) vs WinUI: default formatter = DateTimeFormatter.ShortDate, overridable via DateFormat (CalendarDatePicker_Partial.cpp:473, :78-80). Fix: CurrentCulture ShortDatePattern default; expose DateFormat override.
- [low|styling-delta] Pressed state: text/border don't change; glyph column not fixed 32px — ours: only fills change on hover/press; glyph in padded row (CalendarDatePicker.cs:40-58) vs WinUI: pressed text=TextFillColorSecondary (:14); pressed border=ControlStrokeColorDefault (:26); glyph column Width=32 MaxWidth=32 (glyph E787 size 12 matches, CalendarDatePicker_themeresources.xaml:214, :219). Fix: PressedBorderColor=StrokeControlDefault, pressed text TextSecondary; fixed 32px trailing glyph column.

### DateTime shared (DatePicker/TimePicker/CalendarDatePicker/CalendarView)

- [medium|styling-delta] Hand cursor on every clickable part; WinUI uses arrow throughout (QUICK) — ours: no Cursor set anywhere in DatePicker.cs/TimePicker.cs/CalendarDatePicker.cs/CalendarView.cs → Reconciler.cs:1001 applies CursorId.Hand to all OnClick nodes (faces, loop rows, step/accept buttons, day cells, nav buttons) vs WinUI: templates define no Hand cursor (DatePicker/TimePicker/CalendarView _themeresources.xaml); hand is hyperlink-only. Fix: Cursor=CursorId.Arrow on every clickable BoxEl in the four controls (override path Reconciler.cs:1106).
- [low|styling-delta] FocusVisualMargin: only CalendarView nav buttons diverge (QUICK) — ours: nothing set, but the engine already defaults FocusVisualMargin to -3 for every focusable (Reconciler.cs:1113: `ii.FocusVisualMargin = b.FocusVisualMargin ?? Edges4.All(-3f)`) — picker faces and day items already match vs WinUI: -3 (DatePicker_themeresources.xaml:139; TimePicker:133; CalendarDatePicker:93; CalendarView day items :249); nav buttons -2 (:78). Fix: set FocusVisualMargin=-2 on CalendarView prev/next buttons only.
- [low|missing-api] No TemplateParts/Parts.Apply restyling seam in any datetime control — ours: no 'PartXxx' consts or Parts.Apply in the four files vs WinUI: named parts HighlightRect/AcceptButton/DismissButton (DatePicker_themeresources.xaml:293,305-306), HeaderButton/PreviousButton/NextButton (CalendarView_themeresources.xaml:681-683), DateText/CalendarGlyph (CalendarDatePicker_themeresources.xaml:218-219). Fix: export Part consts (PartFace, PartHighlight, PartAcceptButton, PartHeaderButton, PartDayCell…) and route through Parts.Apply per repo convention.

**Do it better**
- [low|improvement] Skip WinUI's MonochromaticOverlayPresenter double-render for highlight text — ours: colors the center row directly (right approach, wrong token — see the highlight-pill finding) (DatePicker.cs:369) vs WinUI: re-renders each selector through a MonochromaticOverlayPresenter purely to tint text (DatePicker_themeresources.xaml:294-296). Keep direct per-row coloring (TextOnAccentAA for the center row); document in control-fidelity.md.

**Effort:** TextBox M (context flyout + v-scroll are the bulk) · NumberBox M · PasswordBox S · ComboBox M · AutoSuggestBox M (chrome rebuild) · Slider M (compensated mapping + IntermediateValue).
RatingControl S · ColorPicker L (axes swap + keyboard + text-input rebuild) · DatePicker M · TimePicker L (structural rebuild) · CalendarView L (API + zoom views) · CalendarDatePicker S · datetime-shared S.

## collections

### ListView / GridView

- [high|styling-delta] Multiple-mode rows show BOTH checkbox and accent pill — ours: pill rendered whenever `selected && enabled`, no mode gate (src/FluentGpu.Controls/ListView.cs:344-363), checkbox renders in Multiple at :324, so both appear vs WinUI: IsInSelectionIndicatorMode true only for SelectionMode Single || Extended; Multiple shows checkbox only (ListViewBaseItemChrome.cpp:1619-1640). Fix: suppress the lv-pill child when `state.ShowCheckbox` (Multiple) and when SelectionMode==None (capture mode in the Chrome closure). (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] ItemClick fires only on pointer Tap — ours: `if (t == ItemContainerTrigger.Tap) onItemClick(item)` (ListView.cs:239-241, GridView.cs:183-185); EnterKey/SpaceKey/DoubleTap never invoke vs WinUI: Enter/Space → OnItemPrimaryInteractionGesture, Ctrl+Space → secondary (ListViewBase_Partial_Interaction.cpp:744-781), both raise OnItemClick when IsItemClickEnabled (:252-266, :343-348). Fix: also call onItemClick for ItemContainerTrigger.EnterKey, SpaceKey (and the second press of a double-click) in both controls. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Selection/click commits on pointer PRESS, not RELEASE — ours: OnPointerPressed fires the interaction immediately (ListView.cs:383-384, GridView.cs:316-317), and this is a self-documented substrate idiom at src/FluentGpu.Controls/ItemContainer.cs:41-45 ("visual outcome is identical" — disproved for slide-off-cancel and drag-start-no-select) vs WinUI: EnqueuePendingTapInteractionForPointerId on press (ListViewBaseItem_Partial.cpp:467/:528), performed on PointerReleased (:858-859), slide-off cancels via CancelPendingTapInteractionForPointerId (:845-847), drag start does not select. Fix: change the documented substrate idiom in ItemContainer.Build + both skins (not per-control patches) — route the Tap trigger through a release/click edge; BoxEl.OnClick exists (src/FluentGpu.Dsl/Element.cs:45). Same change covers ic-press-06 below.
- [medium|styling-delta] Missing 7px content prefix + 83ms slide in selection-indicator mode — ours: contentLeft = 16 (+28 only for checkbox), no indicator-mode offset (ListView.cs:304) vs WinUI: contentPrefixWidth = 4+3+0 = 7 for ALL items when SelectionMode Single/Extended (ListViewBaseItemChrome.cpp:2431-2438/:2542-2559; Inline is the idl default, controls2.idl:379-383); mode enter/exit slides content 83ms (Partial.cpp:743). Fix: in Single/Extended add a 7px content prefix to every row (contentLeft 23) with the 83ms slide on mode change.
- [medium|motion-delta] Multi-select checkbox slide uses legacy 333ms/0.1,0.9,0.2,1 — ours: MultiSelectAnimMs=333 + Easing.FluentDecelerate both directions (ListView.cs:50, :320, :334-338); checkbox slides from −28 vs WinUI rounded chrome: entering 250ms spline(0,0,0,1), exiting 167ms spline cp2=(1,0) cp3=(1,1) (ListViewBaseItemPresenter_Partial.cpp:524-541; 333ms is the non-rounded path :545-549); checkbox translates by 20 (chrome cpp:3064), content by 28. Fix: enter 250ms spline 0,0,0,1; exit 167ms ease-in spline 1,0,1,1; checkbox slide distance 20, content 28. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-api] ListViewBase surface gaps — ours: Header/Footer, IsMultiSelectCheckBoxEnabled absent (searched ListView.cs/GridView.cs/ItemsView.cs); SingleSelectionFollowsFocus only on SelectionModel.cs:75 via custom model vs WinUI: ListViewBase Header/Footer + HeaderTemplate, IsMultiSelectCheckBoxEnabled, SingleSelectionFollowsFocus (ListViewBase_Partial.cpp surface; grouping/SemanticZoom intentionally out of scope). Fix: add Header/Footer element props on ListView/GridView; bool props forwarding to ShowCheckbox gating and SelectionModel.SingleSelectionFollowsFocus.
- [medium|bug] GridView double-counts the 4px gap (~8px spacing, shrunken plates) — ours: RepeatLayout.Grid(columns, TileSize, ItemGap=4) at GridView.cs:216 (VirtualLayout.cs:98/:117-122 already spaces cells by Gap) plus Margin(0,0,4,4) inside the cell at GridView.cs:298, shrinking the plate 4px each axis vs WinUI: Margin 0,0,4,4 is the ONLY spacing (GridViewItem_themeresources.xaml:144); net tile-to-tile gap is 4. Fix: pass gap 0 to RepeatLayout.Grid and let the 0,0,4,4 margin be the spacing (stride/content-extent math updated), or drop the tile margin.
- [low|motion-delta] Pill disappears instantly on deselect — ours: LayoutTransition has Enter only (Sy:0, Opacity:0), no Exit (ListView.cs:358-361) vs WinUI: deselect registers opacity→0 over 83ms, no scale on hide (ListViewBaseItemPresenter_Partial.cpp:945-955). Fix: add `Exit: new EnterExit(Opacity: 0f, Active: true)` with ~83ms opacity tween. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Pill height fixed at 16 — ours: Height = 16f, AlignSelf Center (ListView.cs:351) vs WinUI: height = MAX(16, availableHeight − 20 − 20) (s_selectionIndicatorMargin {4,20,0,20}, ListViewBaseItemChrome.cpp:1752-1757/:58). Fix: pill height = max(16, rowHeight − 40); identical at the default 40px MinHeight. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Disabled+selected chrome dropped (merged lv-08 + gv-03) — ours: ListView pill omitted when disabled (`if (selected && enabled)`, ListView.cs:344); GridView 1px inner ControlSolid ring omitted when disabled (GridView.cs:261; outer AccentDisabled border kept :308) vs WinUI: ListViewItemSelectionIndicatorDisabledBrush = AccentFillColorDisabledBrush (ListViewItem_themeresources.xaml:78); inner selection border removed only when !selected, SelectedDisabledBorderBrush exists (ListViewBaseItemChrome.cpp:2994-3001, :30).
