- [low|styling-delta] Check plate hover/press/disabled ramps missing (merged lv-09 + gv-02) — ours: ListView checked fill/border always Tok.AccentDefault, glyph always TextOnAccentPrimary (ListView.cs:405-410, :425); GridView unchecked plate always Tok.FillControlOnImage, border always StrokeControlStrongDefault (GridView.cs:337-342) vs WinUI: CheckBoxSelectedPointerOver=AccentFillColorSecondary, SelectedPressed=AccentFillColorTertiary, CheckPressed=TextOnAccentFillColorSecondary (ListViewItem_themeresources.xaml:67/:68/:61); GridView CheckBoxPointerOver=ControlOnImageFillColorSecondary, Pressed=ControlOnImageFillColorTertiary, Disabled=ControlOnImageFillColorDisabled, pressed border=ControlStrongStrokeColorDisabled, checked ramp AccentSecondary/AccentTertiary (GridViewItem_themeresources.xaml:34/:35/:36/:43/:38-39). Fix: add HoverFill/PressedFill ramps (ControlOnImage Secondary/Tertiary unchecked; Accent Secondary/Tertiary checked), glyph PressedColor TextOnAccentSecondary, and the disabled plate brush. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Item minimum sizes not enforced — ours: only MinHeight=40 (ListView.cs:368); GridView BuildTile sets no MinWidth/MinHeight (GridView.cs:295-325) vs WinUI: ListViewItemMinWidth=88 (ListViewItem_themeresources.xaml:13); GridViewItemMinWidth/MinHeight=44 (generic.xaml:109-110). Fix: MinWidth 88 in BuildRow; MinWidth/MinHeight 44 in BuildTile. (QUICK)
- [low|bug] ItemInvoked/selection indices bypass the live-reorder slot projection — ours: OnItemInvoked/selection passed raw while itemTemplate/itemText/keyOf project through slotsLocal (ListView.cs:273-274, GridView.cs:219-220) — during drag a slot index ≠ item index reaches the app vs WinUI: indices reported in data order during live reorder (ListViewBase_Partial_Reorder.cpp). Fix: wrap itemInvoked as `i => OnItemInvoked(slotsLocal[i])` (and consider mapping selection callbacks). (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] Overlay check fade 167ms FluentDecelerate vs theme fade — ours: Tween(167f, Easing.FluentDecelerate) enter+exit on the corner check (GridView.cs:286-290) vs WinUI: TAS_FADEIN/TAS_FADEOUT theme animations (ListViewBaseItemPresenter_Partial.cpp:591-602; PVL timings not pinned). Fix: match the theme-fade durations once pinned; opacity-only fade is correct.

**Do it better:**
- [low|improvement] Typeahead (prefix jump) — ours has it (ItemsView.cs:429-452: printable chars accumulate, 1s reset, wrapping prefix match; inherited via ItemText), WinUI ListView has none (ListViewBase_Partial_Interaction.cpp keyboard path :739-877 only). Keep; document as deliberate improvement.

### ItemsView / ItemContainer / ItemsRepeater

- [high|missing-behavior] No TabNavigation=Once — ours: `Focusable = true` on every container (ItemContainer.cs:161), no TabStop management in ItemsView.cs vs WinUI: ItemsView.xaml:7 TabNavigation="Once"; GettingFocus redirects tab-in to the current element (or selected item when Single+Once) (ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:645-721). Fix: roving single tab stop — TabStop=true only on the keyboard-current container, false on the rest (the RadioButton.cs:205 pattern); on tab-in land on current/selected, not document-order first.
- [high|styling-delta] Hover/pressed fills render UNDER item content — ours: HoverFill/PressedFill on the root BoxEl background plane, beneath the 'ic-content' child (ItemContainer.cs:156-158, :99) vs WinUI: pointer states set PART_CommonVisual.Fill, a Rectangle declared after the child placeholder (ItemContainer.xaml:17-33, :127-135; child inserted at index 0, ItemContainer.cpp:66) so the fill overlays content. Fix: add a full-stretch non-hit-test overlay box ABOVE ic-content carrying SubtleFillColorSecondary/Tertiary hover/pressed fills (visible over opaque photo-wall content).
- [medium|bug] pendingFocus leaks when MoveCurrent targets the already-current index — ours: pendingFocus.Value=next set before the branch; the `else FocusIndex(next)` path never clears it (ItemsView.cs:309-317); UseLayoutEffect (:482-486) later fires on any current change (e.g. clicking another item, :459) and calls FocusIndex(stale, visual:true) vs WinUI: no deferred-focus latch; SetFocusElementIndex focuses synchronously (ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:1314-1354). Fix: in the else branch set pendingFocus.Value = -1 before FocusIndex (or only set pendingFocus when current actually changes). (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] PageUp/PageDown not railed to the current column, no edge-first two-phase — ours: always offsets one viewport and takes layout.Window's FIRST index (`out int f`), so a grid lands in column 0 and a mid-viewport current always jumps a full page (ItemsView.cs:412-425) vs WinUI: phase 1 targets the current page edge; railing via keyboardNavigationReference keeps the same column (ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:1103-1242, :1110-1127); phase 2 page-jumps, phase 3 unrails at list ends. Fix: phase 1 move to nearest focusable item at the current viewport edge in the SAME column (use the current item's cross-axis center); only page-jump when already at the edge.
- [medium|missing-behavior] Arrow/Home/End don't skip disabled items (and select them) — ours: NavigateIndex (ItemsView.cs:319-344) and Home/End (:394-401) never consult IsItemEnabled; MoveCurrent (:309-317) runs model.OnFocusedAction on the disabled index vs WinUI: SharedHelpers::IsFocusableElement gates every adjacent walk (ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:203, :321); Home/End use FindFirst/LastFocusableElement (:1028). Fix: skip indices where IsItemEnabled?.Invoke(i)==false in NavigateIndex/NavigateGeometric; walk inward from 0/count-1 for Home/End.
- [medium|missing-api] No ItemTransitionProvider equivalent — adds/removes/moves never animate — ours: VirtualListEl built with no transition (ItemsView.cs:511-529); ItemCollectionTransition exists only on Repeater.ItemsRepeater (Repeater.cs:100-106) vs WinUI: ItemsView.idl:45 ItemCollectionTransitionProvider ItemTransitionProvider, template-bound to the repeater (ItemsView.xaml:30). Fix: add `ItemCollectionTransition? Transition` to ItemsView.Create; wrap containerTemplate with Repeater.WrapTransition's spec (167ms FluentDecelerate FLIP/opacity).
- [low|missing-behavior] Selection fires at pointer-PRESS, WinUI at RELEASE (cancelable) — ours: OnPointerPressed → Tap trigger → OnInteractedAction, self-documented deviation (ItemContainer.cs:165-170, :41-45) vs WinUI: ProcessInteraction runs on PointerReleased only (ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:831-834); ItemContainer.cpp:446-493 raises on release; PointerCanceled/CaptureLost abort without selecting (:495-511). Fix: move selection to a release-over-item edge (press-drag-off or Esc-cancel must not change selection); keep press for visuals/current. Same substrate change as lv-03.
- [low|missing-behavior] Clicking a partially-visible item doesn't bring it fully into view — ours: OnItemInteraction sets current + selector, never calls BringIntoView (ItemsView.cs:456-470) vs WinUI: pointer interaction calls SetCurrentElementIndex(..., startBringIntoView=true) → StartBringIntoView (ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:894-895, :1340-1345). Fix: call BringIntoView(i, float.NaN) at the top of OnItemInteraction (minimal-scroll mode already matches). (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] SelectedNormal ring should be instant; Disabled should fade 167ms — ours: ring always enter-fades 167ms (ItemContainer.cs:113-116, self-documented :103-105); disabled opacity 0.3 applied instantly (:159) vs WinUI: SelectedNormal DoubleAnimation Duration="0" To="1" (ItemContainer.xaml:37); only SelectedPointerOver/Pressed fade (:54-56, :73-75); Disabled animates opacity→ItemContainerDisabledOpacity over ControlFastAnimationDuration KeySpline 0,0,0,1 (:104-107). Fix: suppress the ring enter tween when not hovered/pressed at mount; tween Opacity to 0.3 over 167ms decelerate on disable.
- [low|styling-delta] Selected inner stroke corner radius shrunk by inset — ours: Corners = InsetCorners(outer, 2) → radius 2 (ItemContainer.cs:126; InsetCorners subtracts at :220-222) vs WinUI: PART_CommonVisual RadiusX/RadiusY bind TemplatedParent CornerRadius via TopLeft/BottomRightCornerRadiusDoubleValueConverter, no inset subtraction → 4 (ItemContainer.xaml:134-135). Fix: use the outer corner radius (4) unshrunk on ic-inner. (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] Checkmark is a static polyline vs AnimatedIcon — ours: PolylineStrokeEl, 3 points, thickness 1.8, 14px box (CheckboxGlyphSize+2) (ItemContainer.cs:202-213) vs WinUI: AnimatedIcon (AnimatedAcceptVisualSource) + FallbackIconSource FontIcon Glyph=CheckBoxCheckedGlyph E73E, FontSize=CheckBoxGlyphSize 12 (ItemContainer_themeresources.xaml:125-134; CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:276, :271). Fix: either accept (deliberate recycle fast path — document) or use Icons glyph E73E at 12px to match fallback geometry.
- [low|bug] Space keypress also feeds typeahead — ours: filter is `e.Codepoint < 32` (space=32 passes) (ItemsView.cs:431); InputDispatcher.cs:796-810 routes chars independently of KeyDown Handled vs WinUI: no typeahead; Space is selection-only (ItemContainer.cpp:549-552, ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:838-841). Fix: ignore codepoint 32 when the typeahead buffer is empty (Win32 list behavior), or skip char 32 entirely in OnRootChar. (QUICK)
- [low|missing-behavior] Double-click in Multiple mode toggles once, WinUI toggles twice (net unchanged) — ours: ItemsView.cs:460-461 skips OnInteractedAction for DoubleTap vs WinUI: each click raises PointerReleased → ProcessInteraction (ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:831-834), MultipleSelector toggles on BOTH releases (MultipleSelector.cpp:55-62); DoubleTap then only invokes. Fix: run OnInteractedAction for the DoubleTap press too (idempotent in Single/Extended). (QUICK)
- [low|missing-api] TryGetItemIndex(viewportRatio) and VerticalScrollController missing — ours: ItemsViewController exposes only Selection/CurrentItemIndex/StartBringItemIntoView/ScrollBy (ItemsView.cs:15-39) vs WinUI: ItemsView.idl:51 TryGetItemIndex(h,v,out index); idl:38 VerticalScrollController (the AnnotatedScrollBar seam); ItemsView.cpp:89-110. Fix: add controller.TryGetItemIndex(hRatio,vRatio) via layout.Window over live ScrollState; expose a scroll-controller hook for AnnotatedScrollBar pairing.
- [low|missing-api] ItemsRepeater element-query trio absent — ours: Repeater.cs:100-166 only count/template/layout + index lifecycle callbacks; no element/node query vs WinUI: ItemsRepeater.idl:183-185 GetElementIndex(element) / TryGetElement(index) / GetOrCreateElement(index). Fix: expose index→NodeHandle query on the realized window (ItemsView.FocusIndex already hand-rolls this walk, ItemsView.cs:261-283) for L4 composers. (ENGINE)
- [low|engine-gap] Overscan is an item COUNT, WinUI cache is viewport MULTIPLES — ours: Overscan=4 items (VirtualListEl.cs:35; Repeater.cs:101) vs WinUI: HorizontalCacheLength/VerticalCacheLength MUX_DEFAULT_VALUE 2.0 per AXIS, split cacheLength/2 viewports per side (ItemsRepeater.idl:174-179; EffectiveViewportScrollViewerTests.cs:345-346) — i.e. 1 viewport before + 1 after per axis. Fix: acceptable perf-budget deviation; optionally support viewport-relative overscan (items = ceil(cacheLength × viewport / itemExtent)). (ENGINE)

**Do it better:**
- [low|improvement] Prefix typeahead (1s reset) — ours: ItemsView.cs:429-452; WinUI ItemsView has none (ItemsViewInteractions.cpp:21-52 only Ctrl+A; IsNavigationKey :596-613). Keep; document as deliberate superset.
- [low|improvement] Range-based selection ops never materialize indices — ours: sorted disjoint ranges, SelectAll one range, InvertSelection complements ranges (SelectionModel.cs:26-27, :169-177, :189-204) vs WinUI: InvertSelection iterates SelectedIndices() per-item IndexPath allocations + per-gap SelectRange (ItemsView.cpp:162-199). Keep — O(ranges), allocation-free; SelectedItems projection stays opt-in (GetSelectedIndices).

### TreeView

- [high|missing-behavior] Drag-drop cannot reparent — ours: ReorderList over SIBLING blocks only; commit = CommitSiblingMove (src/FluentGpu.Controls/TreeView.cs:33-36, :307-322) vs WinUI: drop on item RemoveAt from old parent + Append to droppedOnNode.Children() (TreeViewItem.cpp:104-114); MoveNodeInto at empty slot, any parent (TreeViewList.cpp:126-152). Fix: add drop-onto-row target (append as child) and let the insertion slot resolve to a different parent, with cycle guard (cpp:155-162 walk-up check).
- [high|missing-api] No programmatic expansion or selection — ours: TreeNode has only Label/Children/IsEnabled (TreeView.cs:11-14); expansion lives in private UseState (:104) keyed by generated ids vs WinUI: TreeViewNode.IsExpanded settable (TreeView.idl:32-33); TreeView.Expand/Collapse (idl:118-119, TreeView.cpp:140-150); SelectAll (idl:120, cpp:152-156); SelectedNode/SelectedNodes/SelectedItem(s) (idl:117, 165-168). Fix: add TreeNode.IsExpanded init (seed/controlled expansion), SelectedNode(s) get/set, and a SelectAll path for multi mode.
- [medium|missing-behavior] Keyboard reorder bound to Ctrl+Up/Down instead of Shift+Alt+direction — ours: `case Keys.Up when e.Ctrl && CanReorderItems` (TreeView.cs:241-242; doc at :27 misclaims Ctrl is WinUI) vs WinUI: `canReorderItems && isDirectionPressed && isShiftPressed && isAltPressed && !isControlPressed` (TreeViewItem.cpp:396); Up|Left and Down|Right both reorder (:605/:620). Fix: trigger on Shift+Alt + Up/Left (backward) / Down/Right (forward); leave Ctrl+arrows unhandled; update the class-doc cite. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] No 1s hover auto-expand of collapsed folders during drag — ours: absent (only ReorderList.ListDwellMs slot dwell, TreeView.cs:109) vs WinUI: c_dragOverInterval = 1000 * 10000 (1s, TreeViewItem.h:14-15); OnDragEnter starts timer (cpp:204-224); OnExpandContentTimerTick expands (cpp:348-362). Fix: while dragging over a collapsed row with children for 1000ms, expand it (and recompute sibling extents).
- [medium|missing-behavior] Multi-select drag of all selected subtrees + count badge missing — ours: StartDrag drags the single pressed row only, no badge (TreeView.cs:307-322) vs WinUI: drags all selected nodes, sets DragItemsCount (TreeViewList.cpp:49-76); MultipleDraggingPrimary + MultiArrangeOverlayTextBorder 20px accent count badge (TreeViewItem.xaml:122-127, :139-141). Fix: in multi mode drag all selected subtree roots; render a 20px accent count badge over the checkbox cell.
- [medium|missing-api] No SelectionMode.None — ours: `public bool IsMultiSelectEnabled` (TreeView.cs:62); Invoke always SelectSingle/ToggleMulti (:192-196) vs WinUI: enum TreeViewSelectionMode {None, Single, Multiple}, default Single (TreeView.idl:6-11, :114-116); None maps to ListViewSelectionMode::None (TreeView.cpp:227-232). Fix: replace bool with SelectionMode {None,Single,Multiple}; in None raise ItemInvoked without selecting.
- [medium|missing-api] No lazy children loading — ours: Expanding is a post-hoc notification inside ToggleExpand (TreeView.cs:67, :184-190); chevron only when Children.Length > 0 (:331, :400) vs WinUI: HasUnrealizedChildren + ItemsSource (TreeView.idl:219-227, the TreeViewItem runtimeclass block); chevron forced visible via GlyphOpacity when HasUnrealizedChildren (TreeViewItem.cpp:342-345); Expanding raised so apps populate children (TreeView.cpp:171-192). Fix: add TreeNode.HasUnrealizedChildren (show chevron on leaf); raise Expanding before flattening.
- [medium|missing-behavior] Row invokes/selects on pointer PRESS — ours: `OnPointerPressed = _ => onInvoke()` (TreeView.cs:469); starting a drag also invokes first vs WinUI: OnItemClick via ListView ItemClick on completed tap/release (TreeView.cpp:159-164); drag does not raise ItemClick. Fix: move onInvoke to OnClick (release over same row); keep cursor Arrow explicitly when switching to OnClick.
- [medium|missing-behavior] Multi mode: any row press cascade-toggles selection — ours: Invoke() does ToggleMulti on row press (TreeView.cs:192-196); checkbox lane HitTestVisible=false (:434) vs WinUI: in Multiple mode list SelectionMode is None (TreeView.cpp:241-245) — row click only raises ItemInvoked; toggling is the CheckBox (TreeViewItem.cpp:411-422) or Space (cpp:54-61). Fix: make the 32px checkbox its own hit target that toggles; row body click raises ItemInvoked only in Multiple mode.
- [medium|styling-delta] Chevron shows Hand cursor — ours: chevron cell sets OnClick without Cursor (TreeView.cs:407); engine defaults clickables to Hand (src/FluentGpu.Reconciler/Reconciler.cs:998-1001) vs WinUI: ExpandCollapseChevron grid has no cursor anywhere (TreeViewItem.xaml:143-146) — arrow default. Fix: set Cursor = CursorId.Arrow on the chevron cell BoxEl. (QUICK)
- [medium|motion-delta] Newly revealed children pop in with no entrance animation — ours: `Animate = LayoutTransition.Slide with { Dynamics = TransitionDynamics.Spring(0.18f, 1f) }` — Slide is Position channel only (TreeView.cs:477; src/FluentGpu.Foundation/LayoutTransition.cs:97), no Enter/Exit vs WinUI: ItemContainerTransitions = ContentThemeTransition + ReorderThemeTransition + EntranceThemeTransition (IsStaggeringEnabled=False) (TreeView.xaml:14-21). Fix: add Enter (small Dy + Opacity 0) to the row LayoutTransition.
- [medium|bug] Reference-keyed ids/handles dictionaries never pruned — ours: ids Dictionary(ReferenceEqualityComparer) (TreeView.cs:103), handles (:107), `ids[n] = id` (:120), no removal; rebuilding Roots each render (idiomatic immutable records) gets fresh ids → state lost + unbounded growth vs WinUI: state keyed on app-owned TreeViewNode objects mutated in place (idl:26-45), identity stable by contract. Fix: prune ids/handles for nodes absent from the current Roots walk, or key by app-provided stable key (optional TreeNode.Key).
- [medium|missing-api] CanDragItems/CanReorderItems default true in WinUI — ours: `public bool CanReorderItems;` defaults false; no CanDragItems (TreeView.cs:69) vs WinUI: `<Setter Property="CanDragItems" Value="True"/><Setter Property="CanReorderItems" Value="True"/>` (TreeView.xaml:11-12; idl:139-142 both default true). Fix: consider defaulting CanReorderItems=true (or document opt-in deviation); add CanDragItems if external drag lands. (QUICK)
- [low|missing-behavior] Chevron toggles on release (OnClick), WinUI on press — ours: `OnClick = onChevron` (TreeView.cs:407) vs WinUI: OnExpandCollapseChevronPointerPressed toggles IsExpanded and sets Handled on PointerPressed (TreeViewItem.cpp:698-707). Fix: toggle in OnPointerPressed and mark handled. (QUICK)
- [low|bug] SelectedDisabled hides the indicator; disabled-fill branch is dead code — ours: indicator only when `isSelected && isEnabled` (TreeView.cs:488), so the `:393 Fill = isEnabled ? Tok.AccentDefault : Tok.TextDisabled` disabled arm never runs vs WinUI: SelectedDisabled sets SelectionIndicator Opacity 1 with TreeViewItemSelectionIndicatorForegroundDisabled = TextFillColorDisabled (TreeViewItem.xaml:84-93; TreeView_themeresources.xaml:36). Fix: render the indicator when isSelected regardless of isEnabled. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Disabled rows dim to 0.3 instead of disabled brushes — ours: DisabledOpacity = 0.3f (TreeView.cs:53, applied :464) vs WinUI: TreeViewItemBackgroundDisabled=SubtleFillColorDisabledBrush, ForegroundDisabled=TextFillColorDisabledBrush (TreeView_themeresources.xaml:8, :16; state xaml:52-61). Fix: use Tok.TextDisabled foreground + SubtleFillColorDisabled background (or document as engine-wide convention).
- [low|styling-delta] Padding deltas (merged tv-pad-14 + tv-multipad-15) — ours: row Padding (depth*IndentStep, 3, 8, 5) — right 8 (TreeView.cs:485); chevron Padding always 14,0,14,0 (:403), no multiselect override vs WinUI: TreeViewItemPresenterPadding 0,3,0,5 — right 0 (TreeView_themeresources.xaml:39; item Padding=0, TreeViewItem.xaml:4); multi-select states set ExpandCollapseChevron.Padding=0,0,14,0 and ContentPresenterGrid.Padding=0 (TreeViewItem.xaml:106-107, :115-116). Fix: right padding 0; when showCheckbox use chevron Padding (0,0,14,0) and drop the 3/5 vertical row padding — content sits 14px left of current. (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] Checkbox lane slide/fade (167ms, Dx −32) is added motion — ours: LayoutTransition Opacity tween 167ms FluentDecelerate with Dx -32 Enter/Exit (TreeView.cs:435-439) vs WinUI: MultiSelectCheckBox.Visibility = Visible plain setter, no storyboard (TreeViewItem.xaml:105/:112). Fix: drop for strict parity or keep and self-document as deliberate polish.
- [low|missing-api] Chevron customization props missing — ours: GlyphSize const 8f (TreeView.cs:52); glyphs hardcoded U+E70D/U+E76C, color Tok.TextPrimary (:410-417) vs WinUI: GlyphOpacity (1.0), GlyphBrush, ExpandedGlyph, CollapsedGlyph, GlyphSize 8.0 all settable (TreeView.idl:198-206). Fix: expose optional glyph/size/color overrides (defaults unchanged). (QUICK)
- [low|missing-api] SelectionChanged reports (node,bool) per gesture root — ours: `Action<TreeNode, bool>? SelectionChanged` invoked once with the toggled root (TreeView.cs:66, :175) vs WinUI: TreeViewSelectionChangedEventArgs {AddedItems, RemovedItems} batching all cascaded items per gesture (TreeView.idl:93-97; ViewModel.cpp:363-384). Fix: pass added/removed lists (all cascaded nodes) per gesture.
- [low|missing-behavior] Left/Right expand-collapse not mirrored for RTL — ours: Left=collapse/parent, Right=expand/child, no flow-direction check (TreeView.cs:265-282) vs WinUI: flowDirectionReversed = (FlowDirection() == RightToLeft) swaps roles (TreeViewItem.cpp:640-675). Fix: swap Left/Right semantics when the engine gains FlowDirection. (ENGINE)

**Do it better:**
- [low|improvement] Live spring drag projection beats WinUI's empty-slot model — ours: subtree block extents + ReorderList live projection (TreeView.cs:297-322); WinUI: discrete m_emptySlotIndex insertion (TreeViewList.cpp:126-152) plus a precedence bug `key == Up || key == Left && position != 0` (TreeViewItem.cpp:605). Keep our projection; when adding Shift+Alt reorder (tv-kbreorder-01), apply the position guard to both keys, fixing WinUI's bug.

### FlipView / SwipeControl

- [high|bug] FlipView nav arrow glyphs swapped — ours: prev gets U+EDDA, next gets U+EDD9 (comment asserts the wrong mapping) (src/FluentGpu.Controls/FlipView.cs:75-77) vs WinUI: HorizontalPreviousTemplate Glyph=EDD9 (ChevronLeftSmall), HorizontalNextTemplate Glyph=EDDA (ChevronRightSmall) (FlipView_themeresources.xaml:193, :145). Fix: swap — left/previous bar glyph = U+EDD9, right/next = U+EDDA. (QUICK)
- [high|missing-behavior] FlipView wraps around; WinUI clamps and hides the end button — ours: setIdx((cur-1+count)%count) / (cur+1)%count, doc :9 "navigation wraps around", both bars always rendered (FlipView.cs:76-77) vs WinUI: MoveNext clamps at nCount-1 (FlipView_Partial.cpp:131-139), MovePrevious at 0 (:165-171); ChangeVisualState collapses prev at index 0 / next at last (nothingPrevious/nothingNext, :1242-1278). Fix: clamp; don't render the prev bar at index 0 or next bar at count-1 (also when count<=1). (QUICK)
- [high|motion-delta] No slide animation between adjacent items — ours: current item swapped instantly in Render(), no offset/keyframe animation (FlipView.cs:69-74) vs WinUI: adjacent index change animates via ScrollViewer.BringIntoViewport DManip inertia curve when UseTouchAnimationsForAllNavigation (default true); non-adjacent or m_skipAnimationOnce jumps via SetOffsetToSelectedIndex (FlipView_Partial.cpp:1643-1699, :1719). Fix: direction-aware horizontal slide for ±1 changes via UseKeyframes(AnimChannel.TranslateX) (note: AnimChannel.TranslateX, src/FluentGpu.Animation/AnimEngine.cs:10 — there is no AnimChannel.X; UseKeyframes pattern at src/FluentGpu.Controls/ProgressRing.cs:120); jump for non-adjacent; gate behind a UseTouchAnimationsForAllNavigation-like flag (default true).
- [high|missing-api] No SelectedIndex/SelectionChanged API; items are strings only — ours: Items is IReadOnlyList<string>, index in private UseState(0), no change callback, no Element content (FlipView.cs:13-22) vs WinUI: FlipView is a Selector — SelectedIndex/SelectionChanged (FlipView_Partial.cpp:129, :1607-1613); arbitrary content via FlipViewItem (FlipViewItem_themeresources.xaml:23-25); UseTouchAnimationsForAllNavigation (:1639). Fix: accept IReadOnlyList<Element> (or item factory), expose SelectedIndex + OnSelectionChanged (controlled or initial-value), plus the animations bool.
- [medium|missing-behavior] Nav buttons always visible — ours: NavBars rendered unconditionally, no hover gating or timer (FlipView.cs:48-58, :76-77) vs WinUI: show on non-touch PointerEntered (touch hides immediately) (FlipView_Partial.cpp:767-774); fade-out timer FLIP_VIEW_BUTTONS_SHOW_DURATION_MS = 3000ms (FlipView_Partial.h:13, cpp:1856); stays visible while pointer over a button (:1174-1175); keyboard focus also shows (:1472-1473). Fix: hide by default; show on pointer enter/move (mouse), keep while hovered, hide 3000ms after last activity, hide immediately on touch.
- [medium|missing-behavior] No mouse-wheel flipping (200ms distinct-delta rule) — ours: absent, only OnClick handlers (FlipView.cs) vs WinUI: OnPointerWheelChanged flips one item per event, allowed on direction change or after FLIP_VIEW_DISTINCT_SCROLL_WHEEL_DELAY_MS = 200ms (s_scrollWheelDelayMS declared FlipView_Partial.h:28, defaults to it at h:10); Ctrl+wheel ignored (:666-668); unhandled at first/last so parent scroll-chains (:736; cpp:650-749). Fix: wheel delta<0 → next, >0 → prev, throttled 200ms unless direction changed; don't consume at ends. (ENGINE — no per-element wheel event exists: no OnWheel in src/FluentGpu.Dsl/Element.cs; src/FluentGpu.Input/InputDispatcher.cs:317-319 routes InputKind.Wheel only to NodeFlags.Scrollable nodes via ScrollAt :412-421.)
- [medium|missing-behavior] No keyboard navigation or focusability — ours: no Focusable/OnKeyDown/FocusVisualMargin, only mouse OnClick (FlipView.cs) vs WinUI: HandleNavigationKey — Left/Up = previous, Right/Down = next (per orientation, RTL-inverted), Home/End = first/last (Selector_Partial.cpp:3694-3769); TabNavigation=Once, IsTabStop=False (FlipView_themeresources.xaml:80-81); keyboard focus shows buttons (FlipView_Partial.cpp:1471-1473). Fix: make the frame Focusable; OnKeyDown maps Left/Up→prev, Right/Down→next, Home→0, End→count-1; show nav bars while keyboard-focused.
- [medium|missing-behavior] No touch/drag panning with mandatory-single snap — ours: no OnDrag/OnPointerDown (FlipView.cs) vs WinUI: ScrollingHost Vertical/HorizontalSnapPointsType=MandatorySingle (FlipView_themeresources.xaml:297); OnScrollViewerViewChanged rounds offset/viewport to nearest index (FlipView_Partial.cpp:441-536). Fix: OnDrag-based horizontal panning of the content layer; on release snap to round(offset/viewport) and commit that index.
- [medium|missing-api] No vertical orientation — ours: no orientation parameter; bars hard-coded left/right (FlipView.cs) vs WinUI: VerticalNext/PreviousTemplate glyphs EDDC (next) / EDDB (prev) (FlipView_themeresources.xaml:200-295); vertical buttons 38x16 at Top/Bottom center (:302-303); scroll mode follows ItemsPanel orientation (FlipView_Partial.cpp:404-415). Fix: orientation option — vertical uses 38x16 top/bottom bars, glyphs U+EDDB (prev) / U+EDDC (next), Up/Down keys.
- [medium|missing-behavior] Arrow doesn't recolor on hover/press; press-scale targets the bar — ours: TextEl Color = Tok.FillControlStrong fixed (FlipView.cs:57); PressScale=0.875f on the whole BoxEl (:52); comment :45-47 claims the recolor but nothing implements it vs WinUI: arrow ControlStrongFillColorDefault → TextFillColorSecondary on PointerOver/Pressed (FlipView_themeresources.xaml:10-12); Pressed scales the Arrow FontIcon (RenderTransform origin 0.5,0.5) by FlipViewButtonScalePressed=0.875 (:133-140, :75); button background never changes. Fix: track hover/press, recolor glyph Tok.FillControlStrong → Tok.TextSecondary; move the 0.875 press scale onto the glyph element, not the 16x38 bar.
- [medium|bug] Nav buttons get Hand cursor — ours: NavBar sets OnClick without Cursor (FlipView.cs:48-58); engine defaults OnClick nodes to Hand (Reconciler.cs:1001) vs WinUI: nav templates are plain Buttons — arrow cursor (FlipView_themeresources.xaml:104-199). Fix: Cursor = CursorId.Arrow on both NavBar BoxEls. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Nav button background should be in-app acrylic — ours: Fill = Tok.FillControlDefault (FlipView.cs:51, substitution documented :45-46) vs WinUI: FlipViewNextPreviousButtonBackground[/PointerOver/Pressed] = AcrylicInAppFillColorDefaultBrush all three states (FlipView_themeresources.xaml:7-9). Fix: use engine acrylic (BoxEl.Acrylic, Reconciler.cs:931; Tok.AcrylicFlyout is the matching AcrylicInAppFillColorDefault token), constant across states. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Frame corner radius 8 vs WinUI 4; bars missing 1px inset (merged fv-12 + fv-13) — ours: Corners = Radii.OverlayAll (=8, Radii.cs:9) (FlipView.cs:30, :63); bars at OffsetX = 0 and Width-BarW, touching the edges (:76-77) vs WinUI: CornerRadius = ControlCornerRadius (=4) (FlipView_themeresources.xaml:98); nav buttons Margin="1" (:300-301). Fix: Radii.ControlAll on the outer frame (bars already use ControlAll — correct); inset bars 1px (OffsetX = 1 / Width-BarW-1, and 1px on vertical centering). (QUICK)
- [high|missing-behavior] SwipeControl has no swipe gesture, open/close, thresholds, or light-dismiss — ours: self-described "no live gesture — renders actions already revealed", static row (SwipeControl.cs:16-18) vs WinUI: open threshold c_ThresholdValue=100px — rests open when |pan| >= min(contentSize, 100) (SwipeControl.cpp:21-22; ConfigurePositionInertiaRestingValues :944-1005), else springs to 0; close on inward movement (UpdateThresholdReached :1630-1639); Close() adds velocity 31 (c_MinimumCloseVelocity, :99-119); tap-outside/Esc dismiss (AttachDismissingHandlers, SwipeControl.h:74-76). Fix: drag-to-reveal — content translates with the pan, clipped reveal underneath; on release rest open if |pan| >= min(items width, 100px) else animate closed; Close() API; tap-outside + key dismiss when open in Reveal mode.
- [high|missing-api] Execute mode missing — ours: 'destructive Color' heuristic stands in; no SwipeMode, no threshold state, colored item bold from the start (SwipeControl.cs:38-40) vs WinUI: SwipeMode Reveal/Execute (SwipeControl.idl:20-24); pre-threshold ControlStrongFillColorDefault on ControlFillColorTertiary → post-threshold TextOnAccentFillColorPrimary on AccentFillColorDefault (SwipeControl_themeresources.xaml:8-11); execute item stretches to control width (SwipeControl.cpp:1289-1292), auto-invokes item 0 when opened (IdleStateEntered :214-218). Fix: add Mode (Reveal/Execute); Execute = single item, width = control width, fill Tok.FillControlTertiary/glyph Tok.FillControlStrong before the 100px threshold, flipping to Tok.AccentDefault/Tok.TextOnAccentPrimary past it, invoking on release.
- [high|missing-api] Swipe items are not invokable — ours: action BoxEl has Role=Button and PressedFill but no OnClick/OnPointerDown (inert; the :53 PressedFill likely never shows); SwipeAction record has no callback (SwipeControl.cs:44-60, :14) vs WinUI: Command/CommandParameter/Invoked/BehaviorOnInvoked (SwipeControl.idl:75-91); InvokeSwipe fires Invoked, executes Command, closes unless RemainOpen (SwipeItem.cpp:24-46); tap invokes (OnItemTapped :110-125). Fix: add Action/OnInvoked + BehaviorOnInvoked (Auto/Close/RemainOpen) to SwipeAction; OnClick on each item with Cursor=CursorId.Arrow; close after invoke unless RemainOpen.
- [medium|missing-api] Only trailing-edge actions — ours: Create(content, actions), single list rendered after content on the right (SwipeControl.cs:21, :34, :63-72) vs WinUI: LeftItems/RightItems/TopItems/BottomItems (SwipeControl.idl:48-51); axis inferred from populated sides, throws if both axes populated (SwipeControl.cpp:1655, :1660-1674). Fix: accept leading+trailing (optionally top/bottom) lists; reveal the side matching drag direction; reject mixed axes.
- [medium|styling-delta] Swipe item fixed 68x40 — ours: Width = 68f, Height = 40f (hard sizes, so AlignItems.Stretch at :66 never applies) (SwipeControl.cs:46-47) vs WinUI: SwipeItemStyle MinWidth=68, Width=Auto, MinHeight=40 (SwipeControl_themeresources.xaml:37-39); horizontal items get Height = control ActualHeight (SwipeControl.cpp:1286-1288). Fix: MinWidth=68/MinHeight=40 semantics — width grows with label, item height stretches to the content cell. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Gallery frame adds border + 4px corners WinUI lacks; reveal background per-item not full-bleed — ours: root Corners=Radii.ControlAll, BorderColor=Tok.StrokeCardDefault, BorderWidth=1; each item carries its own fill (SwipeControl.cs:63-72, :39, :52) vs WinUI: RootGrid bare (SwipeControl.xaml:11-19); reveal paints SwipeContentRoot with SwipeItemBackground full-bleed, outermost custom item Background bleeds across (SwipeControl.cpp:1398-1439). Fix: drop (or self-document) the demo border/corners; paint one SwipeItemBackground plate under all reveal items.

**Do it better:**
- [low|improvement] Smooth precision-touchpad paging instead of WinUI's 200ms flip throttle — WinUI self-documents the weakness (touchpad flicks spread wheel deltas over seconds, "may require the user to wait a few seconds", FlipView_Partial.cpp:708-712). When implementing fv-05/fv-07, treat continuous touchpad deltas as a tracked pan with snap-on-settle — strictly better feel.

### ScrollBar / AnnotatedScrollBar

- [high|styling-delta] ScrollBar arrow buttons show Hand cursor — ours: arrow cell sets OnClick with no Cursor (src/FluentGpu.Controls/ScrollBar.cs:426-454); Reconciler.cs:1001 defaults clickables to CursorId.Hand vs WinUI: template arrows are RepeatButtons with no cursor override — system arrow (ScrollBar_themeresources.xaml:703/:711). Fix: Cursor = CursorId.Arrow on both arrow cells (explicit override beats the hand default, Reconciler.cs:1106). (QUICK)
- [high|missing-behavior] Bar contracts mid-drag when pointer drifts off the 12px lane — ours: LaneLeave starts the 500ms contract dwell unconditionally (ScrollBar.cs:389-397); InputDispatcher.cs:178/:636 reassigns hover and fires OnPointerExit even during a live OnDrag gesture vs WinUI: OnPointerExited sets m_isPointerOver=FALSE but skips UpdateVisualState while IsDragging — bar stays Expanded until the thumb drag ends (ScrollBar_Partial.cpp:548-561). Fix: gate LaneLeave while dragging.Value (defer the flip; re-evaluate hover at drag end). (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Track-click pages once; WinUI auto-repeats while held — ours: StripDown fires one page jump per press; strip has no Repeats (only arrow cells set Repeats=true) (ScrollBar.cs:224-237, :436) vs WinUI: VerticalLargeDecrease/LargeIncrease are RepeatButtons Interval=50 (ScrollBar_themeresources.xaml:704/:710) — paging stops when the thumb reaches the pointer. Fix: arm repeat on track press (500ms delay then repeat), re-evaluating pointer side and stopping when the thumb passes it.
- [medium|missing-behavior] Page amount is viewport*0.875; LargeChange not exposed — ours: page = fraction*0.875/(1-fraction) (ScrollBar.cs:216); no LargeChange on Anatomy (:147-148) vs WinUI: LargeDecrement → IScrollInfo::PageUp → SetVerticalOffset(offset - viewport) (ScrollViewer_Partial.cpp:3146-3147; ScrollContentPresenter_Partial.cpp:543-547). Fix: drop the 0.875 factor (page = fraction/(1-fraction) normalized); expose optional largeChange override. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Arrow step is page/8 (~viewport*0.11); WinUI line-scrolls 16px — ours: small = page / 8f, no smallChange parameter (ScrollBar.cs:217) vs WinUI: ScrollViewerLineDelta = 16.0f px per arrow click (dxaml/xcp/dxaml/lib/ScrollViewer_Partial.h:27; SetVerticalOffset(offset - ScrollViewerLineDelta) in LineUpImpl/LineDownImpl, dxaml/xcp/dxaml/lib/ScrollContentPresenter_Partial.cpp:442/:467). Fix: accept a smallChange01 (callers pass 16/scrollableExtent); default closer to a 16px line than page/8.
- [medium|missing-api] No horizontal orientation on either ScrollBar surface — ours: Anatomy is vertical-only (Width=rail, flex column, Y-only TransformBind) (ScrollBar.cs:147-157; Create :99-127) vs WinUI: full HorizontalRoot anatomy with own thumb/arrows/track (ScrollBar_themeresources.xaml:672-693), glyphs EDDA/EDD9 (:258/:301). Fix: add an orientation parameter mirroring the vertical anatomy on the X axis (glyphs EDD9 left / EDDA right). <!-- canon-allow: historical pre-unification spelling -->
- [medium|styling-delta] AnnotatedScrollBar scroll buttons show Hand cursor — ours: ScrollButton sets OnClick with no Cursor (AnnotatedScrollBar.cs:308-334); Reconciler.cs:1001 defaults to Hand vs WinUI: ScrollButtonStyle RepeatButtons, no cursor override (AnnotatedScrollBar.xaml:31-39/:94-102). Fix: Cursor = CursorId.Arrow on the ScrollButton BoxEl. (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] Detail tooltip right-aligned; WinUI centers it on the 1px tooltip rail — ours: chip row Justify=End (flush right) with OffsetY = hoverY - TooltipMinHeight - 4 (invented 4px gap, assumes MinHeight-tall chip) (AnnotatedScrollBar.cs:218-242) vs WinUI: PlacementRect horizontal = -tooltipWidth/2 + 2 relative to the right rail, Placement=Top at the pointer offset (AnnotatedScrollBar.cpp:559-566; xaml:46-54). Fix: center the chip on the control's right edge (offsetX = -chipWidth/2 + 2), anchor its bottom at hoverY using measured height.
- [low|motion-delta] Arrow auto-repeat interval 33ms vs template Interval=50 — ours: RepeatTicker.cs:26-27 fixed InitialDelayMs=500/IntervalMs=33 engine-wide; BoxEl.Repeats has no per-node interval (Element.cs:105); self-noted at ScrollBar.cs:143-144 vs WinUI: every scrollbar RepeatButton sets Interval=50 explicitly (ScrollBar_themeresources.xaml:681, :703, :711); 33ms is only the plain-RepeatButton default (DependencyProperty.cpp:718-720). Fix: per-node repeat interval (e.g. BoxEl.RepeatIntervalMs) honored by RepeatTicker; scrollbar arrows pass 50. (ENGINE)
- [low|styling-delta] Disabled mouse thumb stays visible — ours: disabled thumb keeps Fill = Tok.FillControlStrongDisabled under root opacity 0.5 (ScrollBar.cs:257, :325) vs WinUI: VerticalThumbTemplate Disabled animates ThumbVisual Opacity to 0 over ScrollBarOpacityChangeDuration 83ms plus the disabled fill (ScrollBar_themeresources.xaml:399-406). Fix: when Disabled, fade/hold the mouse thumb at opacity 0. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Legacy panning variant wrong metrics — ours: Style defaults ThumbWidth=8, MinThumb=30, ThumbHoverScale/PressScale=1.15 (ScrollBar.cs:76-84, applied :111-112); class doc :12-13 claims it mirrors VerticalPanningThumb vs WinUI: VerticalPanningThumb Width=2, MinHeight=32, Margin=2,0,2,0, no hover/press states (ScrollBar_themeresources.xaml:713-714). Fix: default the panning variant to 2px width / 32 min length / 2px side margins, drop the 1.15 scales (or stop citing it as the panning thumb). (QUICK)
- [low|missing-behavior] Anatomy never switches to the touch panning indicator — ours: Anatomy always renders the mouse anatomy; no IndicatorMode/input-device switch (panning visual only as the separate Create surface, ScrollBar.cs:96-127) vs WinUI: ScrollingIndicatorStates TouchIndicator/MouseIndicator/NoIndicator swap roots by last input device (ScrollBar_themeresources.xaml:446-527; ScrollBar_Partial.cpp:722-737). Fix: optional indicatorMode parameter (or engine last-input-kind signal).
- [low|missing-behavior] ASB SmallChange fixed 0.05 vs auto ViewportSize/8 — ours: smallChange01 default 0.05, no viewport input (AnnotatedScrollBar.cs:105/:129, self-noted :96-97) vs WinUI: EnsureSmallChangeValue: SmallChange(ViewportSize()/8) when unset (AnnotatedScrollBar.cpp:484-489; s_defaultViewportToSmallChangeRatio=8.0, AnnotatedScrollBar.h:206). Fix: accept optional viewportFraction, default smallChange01 = fraction/8. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] ASB detail label Bold vs SemiBold — ours: TextEl { Size=14, Bold=true } (AnnotatedScrollBar.cs:239); TextEl exposes only bool Bold (Element.cs:302) vs WinUI: BaseTextBlockStyle FontSize 14, FontWeight SemiBold (TextBlock_themeresources.xaml:10-13; AnnotatedScrollBar.xaml:63). Fix: add a font-weight value (600) to TextEl/text pipeline; use SemiBold for the detail chip. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-api] ASB labels/detail are string-only — ours: annotations = IReadOnlyList<(string Label, float Position01)>; detailLabel = Func<float,string> (AnnotatedScrollBar.cs:101, :107) vs WinUI: Labels = IVector<AnnotatedScrollBarLabel(Object content, Double scrollOffset)> with LabelTemplate/DetailLabelTemplate IElementFactory (AnnotatedScrollBar.idl:33-39, :51-53). Fix: accept Element (or Func<.,Element>) label/detail factories alongside the string overloads.

**Do it better:**
- [low|improvement] Signal-bound thumb avoids WinUI's per-tick dependent-animation relayout — ours: thumb position is a compositor TransformBind, 2-6px expand a WidthBind signal (ScrollBar.cs:248-261); WinUI's template admits the width expand needs an EnableDependentAnimation keyframe rerasterizing rounded corners every tick (ScrollBar_themeresources.xaml:585-588). Keep; note in the fidelity doc as a deliberate engine win. <!-- canon-allow: historical pre-unification spelling -->

**Effort:** listview-gridview M (mostly token/duration/gating tweaks + the shared ItemContainer release-edge substrate change + Header/Footer API); itemsview-repeater M (roving tab stop, overlay fill plane, nav/paging fixes; 2 small ENGINE items); treeview L (drag reparent + hover-expand + multi-drag, SelectionMode/programmatic expand-select API, id pruning).
flipview-swipe L (FlipView needs slide motion, keyboard, wheel (ENGINE hook), panning, Selector-style API; SwipeControl needs the entire gesture/Execute/invoke build); scrollbars M (4 QUICK cursor/gating/paging fixes + repeat semantics + horizontal anatomy; 2 small ENGINE items: per-node repeat interval, TextEl font weight 600).

## navigation-chrome

Paths below: ours are relative to `C:\WAVEE\fluent-gpu` (controls in `src/FluentGpu.Controls/`), WinUI references relative to `C:\WAVEE\microsoft-ui-xaml` (`controls/dev/...`, `dxaml/...`).

### NavigationView

- [high|bug] Child indentation 24px vs WinUI 31px/level — ours: `const float IndentStep = 24f` (NavigationView.cs:815) vs WinUI: `static constexpr int c_itemIndentation = 31` (NavigationViewItemBase.h:63, applied `Depth() * c_itemIndentation` NavigationViewItem.cpp:899). Fix: `IndentStep = 31f`. (QUICK)
- [high|bug] Hand cursor on all nav elements; WinUI uses arrow everywhere — ours: zero `Cursor` settings in NavigationView.cs; every OnClick node gets Hand via Reconciler.cs:998-1001 default (item rows :961, toggle/back/search :810, top items :738, overflow button :674, overflow flyout rows :637, scrim :378) vs WinUI: no cursor anywhere in controls/dev/NavigationView (arrow default; hand is hyperlink-only). Fix: set `Cursor = CursorId.Arrow` on every clickable BoxEl. (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] Indent shifts whole row (backplate) instead of content only — ours: row Margin left = ItemMarginX + depth*IndentStep (NavigationView.cs:951), so hover/selected backplate narrows per depth vs WinUI: UpdateContentLeftIndentation sets ContentGrid.Margin.Left only; LayoutRoot backplate stays full pane width (NavigationViewItemPresenter.cpp:264-277, themeresources:451). - [medium|styling-delta] Item vertical margin 0 vs WinUI 2 (row pitch 36 vs 40) — ours: `ItemMarginY = 0f` (NavigationView.cs:176; row margin :951, SelectedY pitch :860 ItemOuterHeight=36) vs WinUI: NavigationViewItemButtonMargin = 4,2 (themeresources:228, applied :451) → 40px pitch. - [medium|styling-delta] Chevron glyphs right/down; WinUI is down⇄up — ours: collapsed=ChevronRight E76C, expanded=ChevronDown E70D, size 8 (NavigationView.cs:977) vs WinUI: fallback glyph E70D size 8 (themeresources:268-269); AnimatedChevronUpDownSmallVisualSource rotates down(collapsed)⇄up(expanded), 12x12 icon in 40px-wide grid (:617-619). - [medium|missing-behavior] Chevron is not a separate hit target — ours: ChevronCell has no OnClick; row click selects AND toggles (NavigationView.cs:971-978, Activate :273-278) vs WinUI: chevron handles its own press/release (NavigationViewItemPresenter.cpp:135-173); release only flips IsExpanded, no invoke/selection (NavigationViewItem.cpp:922-925). - [medium|missing-behavior] No indicator on collapsed ancestor of selected item — ours: SelectedY walks only visible flat rows, returns -1000 (pill fades out) when selection is inside a collapsed group (NavigationView.cs:841-864) vs WinUI: FindLowestLevelContainerToDisplaySelectionIndicator animates the indicator onto the collapsed parent (NavigationView.cpp:5553-5584, :5597-5607). - [medium|motion-delta] Indicator move not animated in top mode or compact rail — ours: top pill is per-item static fill; CompactPane rows use static ownIndicator sliver (:915, :545); sliding NavIndicator only mounts in FullPane (NavigationView.cs:493, :737/:757-764) vs WinUI: top animates Offset.X/Scale.X/CenterPoint.X (NavigationView.cpp:2223-2227); compact rail uses the same left-nav Offset.Y animation (:2229-2234). Fix: reuse a NavIndicator-style overlay (X-spring for top, Y-spring for rail) instead of per-item fills.
- [medium|motion-delta] Pane open/close motion symmetric spring vs WinUI 350ms open / 120ms close — ours: PaneTransition Spring(0.22,0.9) both directions; content Slide same spring (NavigationView.cs:155-156, :449) vs WinUI: open SplineDoubleKeyFrame 0:0:0.35 KeySpline 0.1,0.9 0.2,1.0; close 0:0:0.12 same spline (NavigationView.xaml:99, :113). Fix: ~350ms decel curve on open, ~120ms on close (or asymmetric spring presets) for pane width + content slide.
- [medium|missing-behavior] No label tooltip on closed-compact rail items — ours: grep ToolTip = 0 hits; CompactPane rows (NavigationView.cs:520-568) show icon only vs WinUI: ShouldEnableToolTip = IsOnLeftNav && m_isClosedCompact → item Content shown as tooltip (NavigationViewItem.cpp:743-747). - [medium|missing-behavior] Children unreachable in compact rail / top mode (no children flyout) — ours: compact group navigates to first child (NavigationView.cs:523-530); TopItem (:712-769) ignores Children entirely vs WinUI: ShouldRepeaterShowInFlyout (NavigationViewItem.cpp:880-883); ChildrenFlyout Placement=RightEdgeAlignedTop (NavigationView.xaml:469), BottomEdgeAlignedLeft in top mode (:452). - [medium|styling-delta] Top-mode selected item gets Secondary backplate; WinUI is transparent — ours: TopItem Fill = sel ? ### TabView

- [high|missing-api] No items/content API — string-list stub — ours: `public IReadOnlyList<string> Tabs = []` (TabView.cs:32); hardcoded placeholder `"Content of {Tabs[sel]}"` (:128) vs WinUI: TabItems/TabItemsSource/TabItemTemplate, SelectedIndex/SelectedItem + SelectionChanged, TabItemsChanged (TabView.idl:113-174); TabViewItem.Header/Content (idl:205-221). Fix: per-tab content Elements (Header + Content), controlled SelectedIndex + OnSelectionChanged; drop the placeholder.
- [high|missing-api] Close button is a stub: no TabCloseRequested, tab never removed, wrong reselect — ours: `close = () => { if (sel >= idx && sel > 0) setSel(sel - 1); }` (TabView.cs:49) — closing the selected tab selects the PREVIOUS tab vs WinUI: TabCloseRequested (TabView.idl:124); IsClosable (TabView.idl:217-219), CloseRequested (TabView.idl:223 — declared inside TabView.idl, there is no TabViewItem.idl); reselect walks AT the removed index, clamp to count-1 then forward with wrap (TabView.cpp:786-812). Fix: OnTabCloseRequested(index) + per-tab IsClosable; app removes; on close of selected, select same index (next tab), clamped.
- [high|bug] Add button permanently inert — owned no-op OnClick — ours: `Action add = () => { };` (TabView.cs:91) and `Parts.Apply(PartAddButton, addButton) with { OnClick = add }` re-asserts the no-op as owned (:105) vs WinUI: IsAddTabButtonVisible, AddTabButtonCommand(+Parameter), AddTabButtonClick (TabView.idl:120-128). Fix: expose OnAddTabButtonClick (+ IsAddTabButtonVisible) wired as the owned OnClick. (QUICK)
- [high|missing-api] No TabWidthMode: Equal (default, clamp 100–240), SizeToContent, Compact — ours: absent; pure content sizing vs WinUI: TabWidthMode default Equal (TabView.idl:105-107); TabViewItemMinWidth=100/MaxWidth=240 (themeresources:243-244); `std::clamp` (TabView.cpp:1205, :1228); Compact = icon-only unselected (xaml:484-490, TabViewItem.cpp:284-295). Fix: TabWidthMode prop; Equal: width = clamp(available/count, 100, 240); SizeToContent: intrinsic; Compact: icon-only unselected.
- [high|missing-behavior] No tab-strip overflow scrolling or scroll buttons — ours: absent; overflowing tabs clip vs WinUI: RepeatButtons Delay=50 Interval=100, glyphs U+EDD9/U+EDDA FontSize 8 (TabViewItemScrollButonFontSize, themeresources:257), 32x24 (:255-256, TabView.xaml:158-166); scroll step 50px (cpp:30); disabled at extremes (cpp:689-734); selected tab auto-scrolled into view (TabViewItem.cpp:153-154, 625-631). Fix: horizontal scroll region; 32x24 repeat scroll buttons (EDD9/EDDA, 8px) when overflowing, ±50px/tick, disable at ends, bring-into-view on selection.
- [high|missing-behavior] No keyboard support: Ctrl+Tab cycle, Ctrl+F4 close, arrow focus chain — ours: no Focusable/OnKeyDown/Accelerator anywhere in TabView.cs; engine accelerator seam exists at src/FluentGpu.Input/InputDispatcher.cs:754-757 but is never wired vs WinUI: Ctrl+F4 / Ctrl+Tab / Ctrl+Shift+Tab accelerators (TabView.cpp:77-98); MoveSelection wraps skipping unfocusable (:1517-1545); RequestCloseCurrentTab (:1547-1561); Left/Right moves focus tab→close→…→add with wrap (:1427-1515, TabViewItem.cpp:578-603). Fix: focusable tab items; Ctrl+Tab/Ctrl+Shift+Tab cycle with wrap; Ctrl+F4 closes if closable; Left/Right walk tabs+close buttons+add button. Note: FocusVisualMargin -3 applies only to close/add/scroll BUTTON styles (TabView.xaml:187, :238, :594), not tab items.
- [high|missing-api] No tab drag reorder (WinUI default ON) or drag events — ours: no CanDrag/Draggable/OnDrag* vs WinUI: CanReorderTabs default TRUE, CanDragTabs, AllowDropTabs (TabView.idl:140-145); TabDragStarting/TabDragCompleted/TabStripDragOver/Drop (:171-174), TabDroppedOutside (:126); drag visual TabViewItemHeaderDragBackground (xaml:554-561); drag-over width hole (cpp:1143-1148). Fix: wire engine Draggable/DropTarget (Element.cs:76-104) for horizontal reorder with drag plate (SolidBackgroundFillColorTertiary, OverlayCornerRadius); expose CanReorderTabs (default true) + callbacks.
- [high|missing-behavior] No vertical separators between unselected tabs — ours: only the horizontal stripDivider (TabView.cs:119) vs WinUI: TabSeparator Width=1, HorizontalAlignment=Right, Margin TabViewItemSeparatorMargin 0,8,0,8 (TabView.xaml:553, themeresources:266), brush TabViewItemSeparator=DividerStrokeColorDefaultBrush (:46); hidden for selected + left-adjacent tab (TabView.cpp:217-231), on hover/press of self (xaml:322, :332) and right neighbor (TabViewItem.cpp:503-536). Fix: 1px Tok.StrokeDividerDefault right-edge separator per tab, 8px top/bottom inset; opacity 0 when selected, left-adjacent to selected, hovered, pressed, or right neighbor hovered.
- [high|styling-delta] Selected tab does not fuse with content: divider runs under it, fills mismatch — ours: full-width stripDivider below ALL headers (TabView.cs:119); selected Fill=Tok.FillCardDefault (~5% white, FromRgba(0xFF,0xFF,0xFF,0x0D), Tokens.cs:312) vs content Fill=Tok.FillSolidBase #202020 (:125) vs WinUI: Selected collapses BottomBorderLine (TabView.xaml:337, cpp:316-318); TabViewItemHeaderBackgroundSelected=SolidBackgroundFillColorTertiaryBrush (themeresources:85) = #282828 dark / #F9F9F9 light (Common_themeresources_any.xaml:70, :274). Fix: use the EXISTING `Tok.FillSolidTertiary` (src/FluentGpu.Dsl/Tokens.cs:188; dark #282828 :319, light #F9F9F9 :407) for BOTH selected plate and content surface; split the divider to skip the selected tab's span.
- [high|styling-delta] Hand cursor over tabs, close and add buttons — ours: no Cursor anywhere in TabView.cs; engine default Hand (Reconciler.cs:1001) vs WinUI: plain Button/Grid parts, arrow cursor (TabView.xaml:41, :562, :576). Fix: `Cursor = CursorId.Arrow` on tab item, close button, add button (cf. Button.cs:178). (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] Selected plate missing 4px curve-out feet, -1px overlap margin, selected padding — ours: plain Radii.OverlayTop, same Padding(8,3,4,3) all states, no overlap/z-order (TabView.cs:72, :74) vs WinUI: Left/RightRadiusRenderArc 4x4 outward paths (TabView.xaml:547-548); TabGeometry 4px curve-outs (TabViewItem.cpp:106-118); TabViewSelectedItemHeaderMargin -1,0,-1,1 + SelectedItemHeaderPadding 9,3,5,4 (themeresources:269, :241); ZIndex 20 selected (TabViewItem.cpp:153). Fix: selected = margin -1,0,-1,1, padding 9,3,5,4, 4px concave bottom-outside fillets, render above neighbors.
- [medium|styling-delta] 4px gap between tabs, wrong strip padding — ours: `Gap = 4f, Padding = new Edges4(8, 6, 8, 0)` (TabView.cs:109-111) vs WinUI: tabs adjacent (overlap -1px, themeresources:269); TabViewHeaderPadding 0,8,0,0 (:239). Fix: Gap=0, strip top padding 8. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-api] No IsClosable or CloseButtonOverlayMode — ours: close button unconditionally rendered (TabView.cs:56-67, matches Auto only) vs WinUI: CloseButtonOverlayMode Auto/OnPointerOver/Always (TabView.idl:15-20); OnPointerOver shows only when selected or hovered (TabViewItem.cpp:251-282); !IsClosable collapses with padding swap to 8,3,8,3 (xaml:498-503, themeresources:254). Fix: per-tab IsClosable + CloseButtonOverlayMode; OnPointerOver = visible iff selected||hover; collapsed → right padding 8.
- [medium|missing-api] No per-tab icon (IconSource) — ours: item children are [label, closeButton] only (TabView.cs:84) vs WinUI: IconSource (TabViewItem.idl:215); 16px Viewbox (TabViewItemHeaderIconSize themeresources:246), Margin 0,0,10,0 (:247), foreground ramp TabViewItemIconForeground* (:17-21). Fix: optional leading icon slot, 16px, 10px right margin, color follows header foreground ramp (TextSecondary rest / TextPrimary selected).
- [medium|missing-behavior] Middle-click does not close a tab (ENGINE) — ours: absent; engine blocks it — InputDispatcher.cs:203 `if (e.Button != 0) break;` and :223 hardcodes Button=0 vs WinUI: pointer capture on MiddleButtonPressed (TabViewItem.cpp:418-425); release closes if IsClosable (:449-462). Fix: route middle press/release to OnPointerPressed (PointerEventArgs.Button=2 exists, Events.cs:61); close closable tab on middle release over it.
- [medium|engine-gap] Selected header not SemiBold (ENGINE) — ours: TextEl exposes only Bold; label rendered regular (TabView.cs:52-53 self-documented) vs WinUI: Selected sets ContentPresenter.FontWeight = SemiBold (TabView.xaml:351). Fix: add FontWeight (at least SemiBold 600) to TextEl/text shaping; use for selected tab label.
- [low|styling-delta] Close button spacing/pressed-foreground — ours: Gap=8 before close (TabView.cs:71); glyph fixed Tok.TextPrimary (:65) vs WinUI: TabViewItemHeaderCloseMargin 4,0,0,0 (themeresources:252); pressed foreground TextFillColorSecondary (:133); hover/pressed fills SubtleSecondary/SubtleTertiary (:126-127) match. Fix: 4px gap; pressed glyph → Tok.TextSecondary. (QUICK)
- [low|styling-delta] Pressed/disabled foreground + hover/pressed fill tokens diverge — ours: HoverFill=FillControlSecondary, PressedFill=FillControlTertiary (TabView.cs:80-81); label never dims on press; no disabled state vs WinUI: PointerOver=LayerOnMicaBaseAltFillColorSecondary, Pressed=LayerOnMicaBaseAltFillColorDefault (themeresources:9-10); pressed foreground=TextFillColorTertiary (:13); disabled=TextFillColorDisabled (:16). Fix: add LayerOnMicaBaseAlt fill tokens; press dims label to Tok.TextTertiary; disabled = TextDisabled + transparent fill.
- [low|styling-delta] Bottom line wrong token; selected missing bottom-4px side border — ours: stripDivider Fill=Tok.StrokeDividerDefault (TabView.cs:119) vs WinUI: TabViewBorderBrush = CardStrokeColorDefault (themeresources:68, :146); selected gets TabViewSelectedItemBorderBrush gradient (bottom 4px only, :72-80), thickness 1,1,1,0 (:268). Fix: divider → Tok.StrokeCardDefault; selected plate gets 1px CardStroke side stubs on its bottom 4px.
- [low|styling-delta] Add button centered; WinUI bottom-aligns — ours: `AlignSelf = FlexAlign.Center` (TabView.cs:96) vs WinUI: VerticalAlignment=Bottom, Padding TabViewItemAddButtonContainerPadding 3,0,0,3 (TabView.xaml:40, themeresources:264). Fix: AlignSelf=End with 3,0,0,3 offset. (QUICK)
- [low|missing-api] No TabStripHeader/TabStripFooter slots — ours: strip children only headers+addButton (TabView.cs:114-116) vs WinUI: TabStripHeader/Footer + templates (TabView.idl:113-117; Left/RightContentPresenter xaml:38, :43). Fix: optional leading/trailing Element slots (footer stretches).
- [low|missing-behavior] No auto tooltips — ours: absent vs WinUI: mouse-placed tooltip = header string (TabViewItem.cpp:348-381); close-button tooltip SR_TabViewCloseButtonTooltipWithKA (TabView.cpp:84, TabViewItem.cpp:72-76). - [low|missing-api] No tab tear-out APIs (ENGINE) — ours: absent vs WinUI: CanTearOutTabs + TabTearOutWindowRequested/TabTearOutRequested/ExternalTornOutTabsDropping/Dropped (TabView.idl:147-157, MUX_PUBLIC_V7). Fix: add once engine supports drag-spawned secondary windows.

**Do it better**
- [low|improvement] Derive separator visibility declaratively — WinUI pokes TabSeparator.Opacity imperatively and admits VisualState "leads to undesired behaviour" (TabView.cpp:199-231, 4 SetTabSeparatorOpacity calls on selection change :294-297). Fix: compute per-index separator opacity from (selected, hovered) in one Render() expression — immune to WinUI's stale-opacity bugs.

### Pivot & SelectorBar

- [high|missing-api] Pivot cannot host real per-tab content — ours: placeholder TextEl `"Content for {Headers[selected]}"` (Pivot.cs:92); `Parts.Apply(PartContent, content) with { Children = content.Children }` (:99) re-asserts the placeholder, blocking injection vs WinUI: ItemsPresenter 'PivotItemPresenter' hosts PivotItem content (Pivot_themeresources.xaml:432); PivotItem Margin = PivotItemMargin 12,0,12,0 (:450, :12). Fix: content API (IReadOnlyList<Element> or Func<int,Element>) rendered in PartContent; content margin 12,0,12,0 not All(8).
- [high|missing-api] Pivot has no SelectedIndex / selection-changed API — ours: UseState(0) owns selection (Pivot.cs:35); no prop/callback; Headers is mount-only vs WinUI: SelectedIndex/SelectedItem DPs + SelectionChanged (Pivot_Partial.h:384 OnSelectedIndexChanged, :375 RaiseOnSelectionChanged). Fix: optional controlled selectedIndex/onSelectionChanged (like SelectorBar.Create), keep uncontrolled default.
- [high|missing-behavior] Pivot keyboard: no Left/Right/Home/End or Ctrl+PageUp/Down; one tab stop per header — ours: headers ARE reachable (engine auto-focusable via Reconciler.cs:1111; Enter/Space activate via InputDispatcher.cs:724-743), but no arrow/Home/End selection movement, no Ctrl+PageUp/PageDown/Ctrl(+Shift)+Tab cycling, and one-stop-per-header vs WinUI: Left/Right/Home/End change selection with wrap (Pivot_Partial.cpp:2939-2982); Ctrl+PageUp/PageDown + Ctrl(+Shift)+Tab cycle (:950-983); ONE tab stop (PivotHeaderItem IsTabStop=False, Pivot_themeresources.xaml:485). Fix: arrow/Home/End selection movement with wrap + Ctrl+PageUp/Down; set TabStop=false on individual headers so the strip is a single stop.
- [high|missing-api] SelectorBarItem Icon not supported — ours: `Create(IReadOnlyList<string> items, ...)` strings only (SelectorBar.cs:22) vs WinUI: IconElement Icon (SelectorBar.idl:20); PART_IconVisual scaled 0.8 (SelectorBar.xaml:181-188, SelectorBarItemIconScale=0.8 themeresources:98), icon margin -2,0 (:30), icon/text spacing 8 (:99). Fix: optional per-item glyph — row [Ui.Icon(glyph, 16*0.8, color), text], gap 8, icon margin -2,0, recolors with state ramps.
- [high|missing-behavior] SelectorBar keyboard: arrows don't move selection; every item a tab stop — ours: items ARE focusable (Reconciler.cs:1111) and Enter/Space select (InputDispatcher.cs:724-743), but Left/Right do nothing (arrows route only to OnKeyDown, InputDispatcher.cs:745-751; directional focus gamepad-only :663-666); one stop per item; no FocusVisualMargin=-2; no auto-select on focus vs WinUI: Left changes SelectedItem — selection follows focus (SelectorBarTests.cs:63-66); TabNavigation=Once (SelectorBar.xaml:13); FocusVisualMargin=-2 (themeresources:34); auto-select on focus (SelectorBar.cpp:98-126). Fix: TabStop=false on all but the selected item (roving), OnKeyDown Left/Right move selection, FocusVisualMargin=-2, auto-select on focus when selected<0.

- [medium|missing-behavior] MenuBar opens on click-release; WinUI opens on pointer press — ours: `OnClick = Toggle` (MenuBar.cs:219) vs WinUI: OnMenuBarItemPointerPressed → ShowMenuFlyout when no flyout open (MenuBarItem.cpp:142-152). - [medium|missing-behavior] Enter/Space-opened MenuBar menu doesn't focus first row (ENGINE) — ours: Toggle() sets KeyboardOpen=false (MenuBar.cs:166-170); focusFirst=keyboard||KeyboardOpen → false (:133). Caveat: the dispatcher consumes Enter (keydown) and Space (keyup) for clickable focused nodes BEFORE OnKeyDown routing (src/FluentGpu.Input/InputDispatcher.cs:724-743 vs :745-751), so an OnKey handler can never see them vs WinUI: Enter/Space/Down all ShowMenuFlyout (MenuBarItem.cpp:158-165); SetInitialFocus→CycleFocus focuses first item (MenuFlyoutPresenter_Partial.cpp:1008-1021). - [low|styling-delta] Toggle/Radio check glyph hover/pressed should go TextPrimary — ours: rest TextSecondary, PressedColor=TextTertiary, no hover color (MenuFlyout.cs:127, :135) vs WinUI: PointerOver CheckGlyph=MenuFlyoutItemForegroundPointerOver (TextPrimary), Pressed=MenuFlyoutSubItemForegroundPressed (TextPrimary) (MenuFlyout_themeresources.xaml:420, :429+:23; RadioMenuFlyoutItem_themeresources.xaml:24, :33). - [low|missing-behavior] Pointer leaving the menu doesn't arm cascade delay-close — ours: delay-close armed only when hovering another ROW of the parent presenter (MenuFlyout.cs:399-403) vs WinUI: mouse OnPointerExited outside owner+sub-menu → DelayCloseSubMenu, 400ms (CascadingMenuHelper.cpp:233-252, :783-790). - [low|missing-behavior] Tab moves focus out of menus; WinUI swallows Tab — ours: menus do NOT run in a focus trap (PopupOptions.FocusTrap defaults false, OverlayHost.cs:56; menu opens pass only Chrome/ConstrainToRootBounds, MenuFlyout.cs:364, MenuBar.cs:148), so Tab moves focus across the whole window vs WinUI: VirtualKey_Tab → handled=true, no movement (MenuFlyoutKeyPressProcess.h:27-30, dxaml/xcp/components/controls/KeyDownUp/inc/). - [low|missing-behavior] Cascade popup misses 4px horizontal overlap onto parent (ENGINE) — ours: OpenSub uses FlyoutPlacement.RightEdgeAlignedTop flush (MenuFlyout.cs:363; no offset knob in PopupOptions) vs WinUI: m_subMenuOverlapPixels=4; subMenuPosition.X += subItemWidth − 4 (CascadingMenuHelper.h:121, cpp:678). - [low|missing-behavior] Pointer-opened menu: WinUI still focuses first item — ours: highlight starts -1 unless FocusFirstOnMount (MenuFlyout.cs:261, :375-383); since menus pass FocusTrap=false, focus never enters the popup on pointer opens (focus enters only under PopupOptions.FocusTrap, OverlayHost.cs:601-607) — first Down is consumed OUTSIDE the presenter (e.g. MenuBar title OnKey, MenuBar.cs:178-184) vs WinUI: OnLoaded/OnGotFocus → SetInitialFocus → CycleFocus first item with the opening FocusState (MenuFlyoutPresenter_Partial.cpp:989-1021). ### CommandBarFlyout

- [high|missing-behavior] Secondary toggle click must close the flyout — ours: Run() returns without Close() for ToggleButton; comment mis-cites "CommandBarFlyout.cpp:335-340" (presenter setup) (CommandBarFlyout.cs:529-532) vs WinUI: toggleButton.Checked AND Unchecked → closeFlyoutFunc = Hide() (CommandBarFlyout.cpp:104-105, :417-419). - [high|missing-behavior] No ExpandedUp: overflow always opens below; whole popup re-places near screen bottom — ours: root column always primaryRow→seam→overflow (CommandBarFlyout.cs:305-321); OverlayHost re-places the grown popup every layout (OverlayHost.cs:524-558), so the bar jumps/flips vs WinUI: shouldExpandUp from available space (CommandBarFlyoutCommandBar.cpp:609-657); ExpandUpOverflowVerticalPosition(−h) (:887); ExpandedUp state, border 1,1,1,0, corner flips (themeresources:837-848, :968, :969-972). Fix: decide expand direction; when up: overflow ABOVE primary row, flip seam/corners (Radii.OverlayBottom on primary, OverlayTop on region), animate TranslateY +h→0; primary row stays anchored.
- [high|bug] Hand cursor on every part (trigger, primary buttons, More, overflow rows) — ours: 0 `Cursor` hits in CommandBarFlyout.cs; engine default Hand (siblings set Arrow: Button.cs:178, ToggleButton.cs:166, IconButton.cs:99) vs WinUI: arrow everywhere (hand hyperlink-only). - [medium|missing-behavior] Primary toggle commands have no checked visuals — ours: PrimaryButton() ignores cmd.Kind/IsChecked (CommandBarFlyout.cs:327-356) vs WinUI: Checked → AppBarButtonInnerBorder.Background = CommandBarFlyoutAppBarButtonBackgroundChecked (AccentFillColorDefault, themeresources:386-405, :24), fg TextOnAccentFillColorPrimary (:28), hover AccentSecondary (:25), pressed AccentTertiary (:26). - [medium|missing-behavior] Primary command click closes the flyout; WinUI only auto-closes secondary — ours: Run() (used by PrimaryButton :346) calls Close() for Kind==Button (CommandBarFlyout.cs:526-533) vs WinUI: close handlers hooked only on SecondaryCommands (CommandBarFlyout.cpp:67-74, :60-157, :398-422). - [medium|motion-delta] Width-expansion animation missing (bar snaps wider) — ours: no width/X animation; primary row restretches instantly (CommandBarFlyout.cs:305-321) vs WinUI: V2 expand storyboard discretely jumps the clip to the MIDPOINT at t=0 then animates the second half — ContentRootClipTransform.X −delta/2 → −delta (i.e. ClipR (collapsedW+expandedW)/2 → expandedW) over ControlNormalAnimationDuration (250ms) ControlFastOutSlowInKeySpline (CommandBarFlyout_themeresources.xaml:776-783; values CommandBarFlyoutCommandBar.cpp:921-923); MoreButtonTransform.X delta/2→0 (:772-775); reverse 167ms (:805-829). Fix: expand = right-edge clip (collapsedW+expandedW)/2→expandedW + MoreButton TranslateX delta/2→0, 250ms spline 0,0,0,1; reverse 167ms.
- [medium|motion-delta] Overflow reveal uses V1 full-height content slide; V2 is half-height clip slide, content static — ours: TranslateY −h→0 + ClipT h→0 (full h; comment cites V1 generic.xaml:17009/17018) (CommandBarFlyout.cs:243-244) vs WinUI: ExpandDownAnimationStartPosition(−h/2) (CommandBarFlyoutCommandBar.cpp:891); OverflowContentRootClipTransform.Y −h/2→0 over 250ms spline 0,0,0,1, NO content translate (themeresources:784-787); collapse 0→−h/2 167ms (:825-829). Fix: drop the content TranslateY; animate only the clip far edge h/2→h (ClipB) 250ms FluentPopOpen; collapse h→h/2 then unmount, 167ms. Durations/spline already correct.
- [medium|motion-delta] Flyout open/close should be an 83ms opacity fade, not the menu clip-unfold — ours: PopupOptions(Chrome: PopupChrome.Flyout) (CommandBarFlyout.cs:152) → menu open = 250ms clip-unfold + TranslateY from 50% (OverlayHost.cs:707-756) vs WinUI: AreOpenCloseAnimationsEnabled(false) (CommandBarFlyout.cpp:44); Opening/ClosingOpacityStoryboard = Opacity 0↔1 over ControlFasterAnimationDuration 83ms (themeresources:655-662; kind detection CommandBarFlyoutCommandBar.cpp:208-225). - [medium|missing-behavior] No keyboard navigation (arrows, Tab group hop, auto-expand) — ours: no OnKeyDown; rows only Focusable with engine Enter/Space vs WinUI: Left/Right cycle primary+MoreButton, Up/Down cycle ALL commands with wrap, auto-opening the overflow (CommandBarFlyoutCommandBar.cpp:1200-1292, :1266-1273); Tab from primary opens overflow + focuses first secondary (:1172-1188); Esc hides whole flyout (:1190-1198 — engine Esc covers this). - [low|improvement] Single-popup inline overflow avoids WinUI's shadow remove/re-add hacks — ours: one FlyoutSurface owns shadow/acrylic for the whole popup (CommandBarFlyout.cs:58-63) vs WinUI: removes presenter ThemeShadow during overflow storyboards, re-adds on Completed ("drop shadows do not play well with clip animations", CommandBarFlyout.cpp:356-390, :259-263; CommandBarFlyoutCommandBar.cpp:1505-1542). **Effort:** NavigationView L, TabView L (least-complete control: items/close/add/keyboard/drag/width-mode/overflow all stubs), CommandBar/AppBar L; CommandBarFlyout M, Menus M, Pivot/SelectorBar M, BreadcrumbBar/PipsPager M.
A cross-cutting quick-win sweep (Arrow cursors, constants 31/40/68, Gap=0, glyph E974/E70D-E70E, token swaps, one-line guards) is ~1 day and clears most high-severity styling bugs across all seven controls.

## surfaces-status-misc

### InfoBar / InfoBadge

- [high|missing-behavior] InfoBar inline-vs-wrapped switch is a char-count heuristic, not measure-based — ours: `const int LongMessageChars = 60`; vertical iff `contentItems <= 1 || (hasAction && hasMessage && message.Length >= 60)` — long title+message w/o action never flips (src/FluentGpu.Controls/InfoBar.cs:176-178) vs WinUI: vertical iff `nItems == 1 || totalWidth > availableSize.Width || heightOfTallestInHorizontal > minHeight` (minHeight = parent MinHeight 48 − panel margin) (controls/dev/InfoBar/InfoBarPanel.cpp:69, :20). Fix: measure-driven orientation — vertical when single item, OR summed horizontal widths (incl. inter-child margins) exceed available width, OR any child measured height > 48; needs a width-aware measure callback. (ENGINE)
- [high|styling-delta] InfoBadge Success/Caution/Critical icon badges: wrong margin + oversized glyph — ours: GlyphSize returns IconGlyphSizeFull=16, ContentMargin 4,0,4,2 for all icon badges (InfoBadge.cs:173-178, :204-210) vs WinUI: SymbolIconSource → 'Icon' state → IconInfoBadgeIconMargin 4,4,4,4, content box 16−4−4 = 8 tall (InfoBadge_themeresources.xaml:122/133/144, :16/:65; InfoBadge.cpp:70-77). Fix: for symbol-default severity icons use margin 4,4,4,4 and glyph target height ~8, not Size 16 + margin 4,0,4,2.
- [medium|missing-api] InfoBar Content/ContentTemplate slot (second row) missing — ours: only title/message/actionButton params (InfoBar.cs:125-136) vs WinUI: `Object Content; DataTemplate ContentTemplate` (InfoBar.idl:94-95); ContentArea ContentPresenter Grid.Row=1 Column=1 (InfoBar.xaml:126); NoBannerContent moves it to row 0 when title/message/action all empty (:86-90). - [medium|missing-api] InfoBar custom IconSource missing — ours: only the severity icon Z-stack (InfoBar.cs:146-160) vs WinUI: `IconSource IconSource` (InfoBar.idl:77); UserIconBox Viewbox Max 16×16, Margin=InfoBarIconMargin (InfoBar.xaml:111); IsIconVisible && IconSource → UserIconVisible (InfoBar.cpp:263). - [medium|bug] InfoBar close button gets Hand cursor — ours: close BoxEl sets OnClick, no Cursor (InfoBar.cs:196-217; Reconciler.cs:1001 defaults OnClick→Hand) vs WinUI: plain Button keeps arrow (InfoBar.xaml:127; cf. - [medium|missing-behavior] HyperlinkButton action slot lacks InfoBar implicit style (−12 left margin + accent foreground) — ours: plain BoxEl wrapper with only orientation margin (InfoBar.cs:271-279, :320-327) vs WinUI: implicit style Margin=InfoBarHyperlinkButtonMargin `-12,0,0,0`, Foreground=AccentTextFillColorPrimaryBrush (InfoBar.xaml:117-122; InfoBar_themeresources.xaml:69, :19/:38). - [medium|engine-gap] InfoBar title Bold (700) instead of SemiBold (600) — ours: `Bold=true`, TextEl exposes only bool Bold (InfoBar.cs:253-257) vs WinUI: InfoBarTitleFontWeight=SemiBold (InfoBar_themeresources.xaml:63, bound at InfoBar.xaml:113). Fix: add numeric FontWeight to TextEl (DirectWrite supports it); set 600. Shared with every SemiBold control. (ENGINE)
- [medium|bug] InfoBadge.Count(−1) renders "-1" text inside 4×4 dot geometry — ours: CountCore returns Dot kind (Height 4, MinWidth 4, corner 2) for −1 yet still adds TextEl Size 11 (InfoBadge.cs:130-152) vs WinUI: Value < −1 throws; −1 with no icon → Dot state, no text (InfoBadge.cpp:44-49, :59-82). - [medium|styling-delta] SystemFillAttention wrong in light theme — ours: `SystemFillAttention => AccentDefault`, light = #005FB8 (src/FluentGpu.Dsl/Tokens.cs:289, :427); affects InfoBar Informational circle (InfoBar.cs:104) + InfoBadge Attention fill (InfoBadge.cs:99) vs WinUI: light SystemFillColorAttentionBrush = base SystemAccentColor (#0078D4-class) (Common_themeresources_any.xaml:369); only dark (:165) uses SystemAccentColorLight2 — our dark #60CDFF (Tokens.cs:339) matches. Fix: give SystemFillAttention its own light value = base SystemAccentColor; keep dark = AccentDefault. (QUICK)
- [low|missing-behavior] Close button has no tooltip — ours: none in InfoBar.cs vs WinUI: localized SR_InfoBarCloseButtonTooltip "Close" attached in OnApplyTemplate (InfoBar.cpp:55-59). Fix: attach ToolTip ("Close") to the close button. (QUICK)
- [low|missing-api] No Opened event; CloseButtonClick folded into cancelable onClose — ours: onClose/onClosing/onClosed only; RaiseClose skips onClose on cancel (InfoBar.cs:125-136, :344-353) vs WinUI: CloseButtonClick fires before Closing, NOT cancelable (InfoBar.idl:99; InfoBar.cpp:81-86); Opened raised when IsOpen→true (idl:103-106; cpp:131). - [low|styling-delta] Root not top-aligned — ours: root BoxEl sets no self-alignment, stretches in a stretching parent (InfoBar.cs:224-236) vs WinUI: ContentRoot Border VerticalAlignment="Top" (InfoBar.xaml:15). **Do it better**

### TeachingTip / ToolTip

- [high|bug] Every tooltipped element gets a hand cursor — ours: ToolTip wrapper BoxEl sets OnClick=Toggle, no Cursor (ToolTip.cs:236; Reconciler.cs:1001 OnClick→Hand; InputDispatcher.cs:649 walk-up only stops at non-Arrow) vs WinUI: ToolTipService never changes the cursor (no cursor code in ToolTipService_Partial.cpp). - [medium|bug] Tooltip re-arms from hover-move and reopens in a loop — ours: OnEnter (wired to OnHoverMove, ToolTip.cs:232) re-arms phase=1 whenever phase==0 — after 5s auto-dismiss/press-dismiss any move inside the target reopens (ToolTip.cs:158-164) vs WinUI: trigger is PointerEntered only; dismissed tooltip needs exit + re-enter (ToolTipService_Partial.cpp:1410-1414). - [medium|missing-behavior] No tooltip safe zone — closes instantly on pointer exit — ours: `OnLeave() => CloseNow()` (ToolTip.cs:167) vs WinUI: open tooltip kept on owner-exit; closed by safe-zone check (owner ∪ tooltip ∪ convex hull) polled at 1s (ToolTipService_Partial.cpp:1433-1453, :1060-1062; ToolTipService_Partial.h:22). - [medium|styling-delta] Top-placement tooltip gap 4px vs WinUI 20px (mouse) / 12px (keyboard) — ours: svc.Open(FlyoutPlacement.Top) → FlyoutMargin = 4 (ToolTip.cs:136-142; FlyoutPositioner.cs:72) vs WinUI: DEFAULT_MOUSE_OFFSET 20 / DEFAULT_KEYBOARD_OFFSET 12 applied via InflateRect on the dock rect (ToolTip_Partial.h:10-11; ToolTip_Partial.cpp:1224-1258, :1275). - [medium|missing-behavior] Legacy click-to-toggle opens tooltip on touch tap — ours: Toggle() opens when phase==0; OnClick=Toggle — touch tap opens instantly (ToolTip.cs:195-200, :236; mouse masked by suppressClick :188-193) vs WinUI: opens via PointerEntered/keyboard focus only; touch uses Touch input-mode timing (ToolTipService_Partial.cpp:1771-1772). Fix: transparent LightDismissLayer over content (Cursor=Arrow) closing on pointer-release; Escape closes; host resize closes; cancelable via PaneClosing.
- [high|motion-delta] No pane open/close animation in any mode — ours: pane subtree appears/disappears in one frame (SplitView.cs:31-39) vs WinUI: overlay open TranslateX −OpenPaneLength→0 0.35s KeySpline 0.1,0.9 0.2,1.0; overlay close 0.12s same spline; inline open 0.2s (content pre-slide 0.19999s) spline 0.0,0.35 0.15,1.0; inline close 0.1s; pane clip counter-translates (generic.xaml:15032-15035, :15158-15160, :15328-15344, :15289-15307, :1305-1307). - [high|missing-api] PaneOpening/PaneOpened/PaneClosing(cancelable)/PaneClosed missing — ours: no callbacks (SplitView.cs:20-21) vs WinUI: four events; PaneClosing cancelable on light dismiss, not on app-initiated close (XCPTypesAutoGen SplitView.cs:82-96, :31-39; core SplitView.cpp:212-244, :434-456; SplitView_Partial.cpp:761-781). - [medium|missing-api] PanePlacement=Right not supported — ours: fixed [paneBox, divider, contentBox] order (SplitView.cs:57-62) vs WinUI: SplitViewPanePlacement{Left,Right}; OpenOverlayRight/OpenInlineRight/ClosedCompactRight states (XCPTypesAutoGen SplitView.cs:11-15; SplitView_Partial.cpp:38-57; generic.xaml:15448-15549). - [medium|styling-delta] Default pane width 240 vs WinUI 320 — ours: `float paneWidth = 240f` (SplitView.cs:20) vs WinUI: SplitViewOpenPaneThemeLength = 320 (generic.xaml:85, :15011; SplitView_themeresources.xaml:5). Fix: default 320f. (QUICK)

### Flyout infrastructure (OverlayHost / GenericFlyout / FlyoutPositioner / Popup)

- [high|missing-behavior] Standard flyouts never take focus on open — ours: focus moved only when e.FocusTrap; GenericFlyout passes FocusTrap:false, and the comment at GenericFlyout.cs:59-61 falsely claims the host moves focus in (OverlayHost.cs:601-607; GenericFlyout.cs:65) vs WinUI: m_shouldTakeFocus (Standard mode) focuses the presenter's first focusable child (FlyoutBase_Partial.cpp:2224-2275, :3924-3925). - [medium|missing-behavior] Tab can escape a light-dismiss flyout — ours: FocusTrap:false → no tab-cycle scope ("Tab can leave", GenericFlyout.cs:61, :65; OverlayHost.cs:601-607) vs WinUI: GetTabStop wraps next/previous to first/last focusable of the popup child when isLightDismiss (Popup_Partial.cpp:508-559). - [medium|missing-api] FlyoutShowMode (Transient / TransientWithDismissOnPointerMoveAway) missing — ours: PopupOptions has only FocusTrap/DismissBehavior/Chrome; scrim always intercepts input (OverlayHost.cs:55-82, :770-784) vs WinUI: Transient = no focus take + overlay input pass-through (FlyoutBase_Partial.cpp:3922-3938); MoveAway hides when pointer >80px away (hidingThreshold 6400) (:2435-2449). Fix: ShowMode in PopupOptions; MoveAway adds a root pointer-move watcher closing at 80px from presenter bounds. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Light dismiss fires on click-release, WinUI on pointer press — ours: scrim OnClick = CloseTop(LightDismiss) (OverlayHost.cs:782) vs WinUI: CPopupRoot::OnPointerPressed closes on pointer-down (Popup.cpp:5196-5204). - [medium|bug] FlyoutButton trigger shows hand cursor + missing brush transition — ours: raw BoxEl with OnClick, no Cursor, no BrushTransitionMs (GenericFlyout.cs:75-93) vs WinUI/our Button convention: Cursor=Arrow explicit + 83ms BrushTransition (Button.cs:169-178). - [medium|bug] Collision resize computed but never applied — tall popups overflow — ours: only place.X/Y/OpensUp/CornerJoin consumed; place.MeasuredW/MeasuredH (ResizeToFit shrink, FlyoutPositioner.cs:149-176) dropped; e.MeasuredW/H overwritten from pre-placement layout (OverlayHost.cs:573-582, :545-546) vs WinUI: ResizeToFit shrinks the presenter; Max W/H clamped to available rect (FlyoutBase_Partial.cpp:648-767, :3394-3398). - [medium|missing-behavior] FlyoutPresenter content does not scroll at max height — ours: plain BoxEl MaxHeight 758, overflow clipped (GenericFlyout.cs:98-108; ScrollEl exists, Element.cs:377-381) vs WinUI: ScrollViewer Auto H/V (FlyoutPresenter_themeresources.xaml:34-38, :44). - [medium|missing-behavior] Default flyout placement BottomLeft; WinUI Flyout defaults Top — ours: GenericFlyout.cs:23 + IOverlayService.Open default BottomLeft (OverlayHost.cs:86) vs WinUI: g_defaultPlacementMode = FlyoutPlacementMode_Top (above, centered) (FlyoutBase_Partial.cpp:62).
