- [medium|motion-delta] PopupThemeTransition slides vertically for Left/Right/Full — ours: Popup open always TranslateY ±50 from e.OpensUp (OverlayHost.cs:666-668) vs WinUI: Left/Right use FromHorizontalOffset ±50 (g_entranceThemeOffset), Full uses 0,0 no slide (FlyoutBase_Partial.cpp:2028-2051). ### PersonPicture

- [high|bug] Initials never centered — ZStack stretches text and pins it top-left (root cause of the broken gallery screenshot) — ours: TextEl (no Width/Height) as direct ZStack child; ArrangeZStack stretches unsized children and always places at padL+mL, Justify ignored (PersonPicture.cs:103-110; src/FluentGpu.Layout/FlexLayout.cs:578-585; glyphs paint from bounds top-left, SceneRecorder.cs:191/:349, D3D12Device.cs:418) vs WinUI: InitialsTextBlock VerticalAlignment="Center" HorizontalAlignment="Center" (PersonPicture.xaml:66); font math already exact (0.42/min1, PersonPicture.cs:43 == PersonPicture.cpp:597). - [medium|styling-delta] Initials + badge text Bold (700) vs SemiBold (600) — ours: Bold=true (PersonPicture.cs:106, :147; bool-only Bold, Element.cs:302; SceneRecorder.cs:349) vs WinUI: FontWeight=SemiBold template-bound to InitialsTextBlock/BadgeNumberTextBlock/BadgeGlyphIcon (PersonPicture.xaml:12, :66, :71, :73). - [medium|missing-api] BadgeImageSource / BadgeWithImageSource missing — ours: only badgeNumber/badgeGlyph (PersonPicture.cs:65-66, :112-114) vs WinUI: BadgeImageSource; BadgingEllipse.Fill=ImageBrush UniformToFill, PersonPictureEllipseBadgeImageSourceStrokeOpacity=1 (PersonPicture.idl:14; PersonPicture.cpp:269-291; PersonPicture.xaml:52-62). - [low|bug] Badge OffsetX comment documents wrong engine behavior — correct only by coincidence — ours: comment claims a "centred ZStack" derivation; engine LEFT-pins ZStack children, so left=0+plate+4=52 matches WinUI's 52 only because plate==size/2 (PersonPicture.cs:150-155; FlexLayout.cs:585) vs WinUI: HorizontalAlignment=Right + Margin right −4 → left = size/2+4 = 52 at 96 (PersonPicture.xaml:68). ### Icons / AnimatedIcon

- [high|missing-api] No AnimatedIcon Source/State marker state machine — ours: entire control is a static Glyph() wrapper with HoverScale/PressScale; ComboBox self-documents "until the real AnimatedIcon state machine lands (Wave 4)" (AnimatedIcon.cs:10-32; ComboBox.cs:454-455) vs WinUI: TransitionStates marker lookup chain `<From>To<To>_Start/_End` pair → end-only cut → start-only cut → transitionName → toState → `*To<state>_End` scan → float-parse → cut to 0 (AnimatedIcon.cpp:315-418; AnimatedIcon.idl:20, :29-31). Fix: implement the marker protocol as a Component: state string + Markers map → play segment via UseKeyframes (linear progress, cut when segment <20ms per AnimatedIcon.cpp:436-444), driving glyph transform or PolylineStrokeEl trim.
- [medium|motion-delta] Invented hover-grow + wrong press timing vs Lottie segments — ours: defaults hoverScale=1.08, pressScale=0.88, 83ms both ways (ControlFasterMs) FluentPopOpen (AnimatedIcon.cs:13; Reconciler.cs:958-959; Element.cs:151) vs WinUI: chevron has NO pointer-over motion (NormalToPointerOver_Start/_End both 0.0, AnimatedChevronDownSmallVisualSource.cpp:475-476); pressed ≈151ms (0.312069 × 483.33ms, :478, c_durationTicks 4833333 :104), release ≈300ms (:483-484); Back/Find DO animate hover (:853-854). Fix: per-source motion profiles — chevron hoverScale 1.0, press 151ms in / 300ms out linear; keep hover-pop only where NormalToPointerOver is non-empty.
- [medium|missing-behavior] DropDownButton/SplitButton chevron has no pressed nudge (ComboBox does) — ours: chevron BoxEls carry no HoverScale/PressScale (DropDownButton.cs:108-123; SplitButton.cs:184-191; ComboBox.cs:463-465 has PressScale 0.85, 83ms) vs WinUI: DropDownButton.xaml:63 sets ChevronIcon AnimatedIcon.State=Pressed → AnimatedChevronDownSmall pressed segment (cpp:477-478); same source as ComboBox (ComboBox_themeresources.xaml:585). Fix: apply the identical PressScale stand-in to DropDownButton/SplitButton/ToggleSplitButton chevrons. (QUICK)
- [low|missing-api] FallbackIconSource absent (we are fallback-only) — ours: Glyph(string glyph,…) IS the fallback (AnimatedIcon.cs:12) vs WinUI: FallbackIconSource applied on Loaded / when no visual; e.g. DropDownButton FontIconSource E96E @8 (AnimatedIcon.idl:23; AnimatedIcon.cpp:105-108, :571-595; DropDownButton.xaml:95-97). Fix: with ai-01, accept (animatedSource, fallbackGlyph).
- [low|missing-api] MirroredWhenRightToLeft / RTL mirroring missing — ours: no FlowDirection anywhere (Slider.cs:27-28 "Wave-6 RTL sweep") vs WinUI: UpdateMirrorTransform sets ScaleX=−1 when RTL && !MirroredWhenRightToLeft, origin 0.5,0.5 (AnimatedIcon.idl:26; AnimatedIcon.cpp:487-507). Fix: land with the Wave-6 RTL sweep. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-behavior] No animation queueing — ours: hover/press tweens retarget immediately (cut) (InteractionAnimator.cs:86-87) vs WinUI: default QueueOne, queueLength 4, speedUpMultiplier 7.0; queues pending state, plays on batch completion (AnimatedIcon.h:74, :83, :95; cpp:226-295, :634-666). Fix: with ai-01, queue one pending transition while playing (length 4), optional 7x speed-up.
- [low|missing-behavior] State protocol only covers PointerOver/Pressed — ours: scale progress from own/ancestor hover-press only; Checked/Expanded morphs bespoke (SceneRecorder.cs:159-168; CheckBox.cs:182-186; Expander.cs:80-82) vs WinUI: OnLoaded inherits ANY ancestor State string (AnimatedIcon.cpp:72-103); actual template state names are NormalOn/NormalOff/PointerOverOn/PressedOn/NormalIndeterminate/PointerOverIndeterminate/PressedIndeterminate (CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:324-562; ItemContainer_themeresources.xaml:100/:116/:125 uses NormalOff/NormalOn; Expander_themeresources.xaml:141-270) — NOT "Checked/Expanded". Fix: generic string-state channel on the AnimatedIcon Component resolving marker segments; bespoke keyframes stay as built-in sources.
- [low|missing-behavior] No uniform stretch-to-available-size layout — ours: fixed Width=Height=size (default 16) (AnimatedIcon.cs:15-16) vs WinUI: Uniform measure/arrange — min scale factor to fit, centered offset = (finalSize − visualSize*scale)/2 (AnimatedIcon.cpp:112-189). Fix: optional — derive size from arranged box when host gives a stretch slot.
- [low|missing-api] Icons.cs missing named consts: Contact E77B, People E716, CheckBoxIndeterminate E9AE — ours: PersonPicture.cs:19-20 embeds E77B/E716 as raw literals; CheckBox dash drawn geometrically (Icons.cs:10-82) vs WinUI: PersonPicture.xaml:33/:41; CheckBoxIndeterminateGlyph = E9AE (CheckBox_themeresources.xaml:277). Fix: add Icons.Contact="\uE77B", Icons.People="\uE716", Icons.CheckboxIndeterminate="\uE9AE"; point PersonPicture at them. (QUICK)

**Do it better**
- [low|improvement] Marker-driven PolylineStrokeEl sources beat WinUI's per-icon Lottie codegen — WinUI ships ~500-1300 lines of generated C++ per icon (AnimatedChevronDownSmallVisualSource.cpp; AnimatedGlobalNavigationButtonVisualSource.cpp:1344+); we already have DrawPolylineStroke with trim (DrawList.cs:17) and CheckBox replays AnimatedAccept without Lottie (CheckBox.cs:102, :182-186). Fix: generalize — data-driven source = polyline path + markers table (exact WinUI marker names/fractions) → trim/transform keyframes; new icons become data.

### Panels (Canvas / RelativePanel / VariableSizedWrapGrid / Viewbox / Border)

- [high|bug] Canvas wrapper stretches auto-sized children to full panel height — ours: wrapper BoxEl sets only OffsetX/OffsetY; AlignItems default Stretch + ZStack fill (Canvas.cs:22-27; Element.cs:219, :175-176) vs WinUI: children measured with infinite constraint, arranged at desired size (canvas.cpp:25-36, :62). Fix: `AlignItems = FlexAlign.Start` on the wrapper, exactly as RelativePanel.cs:29 already does. (QUICK)
- [high|missing-behavior] RelativePanel has no constraint system — it is a second Canvas — ours: accepts pre-resolved absolute (X, Y); no RightOf/Above/AlignLeftWith/AlignTopWithPanel/AlignHorizontalCenterWith; panel size caller-fixed (RelativePanel.cs:8, :19) vs WinUI: GenerateGraph + MeasureNodes + CalculateDesiredSize; recursive resolve of the 10 dependency node types (RelativePanel.cpp:30-40; RPGraph.cpp:1126-1139). Fix: implement the RPGraph dependency walk: per-child constraint records, recursive sibling resolve, panel desired size; needs a measure seam to read sibling natural sizes. (ENGINE)
- [high|missing-behavior] VSWG fill direction wrong — WinUI default Orientation=Vertical fills column-major — ours: always row-major left-to-right then wrap down, no Orientation param (VariableSizedWrapGrid.cs:28-44) vs WinUI: default Orientation_Vertical; fill advances row-within-column then next column, rect Y=height*rowIndex, X=width*colIndex (VariableSizedWrapGrid_Partial.cpp:93; VariableSizedWrapGrid_OccupancyMap.cpp:384-388, :347-348). Fix: add Orientation (default Vertical = column-major); current behavior becomes Orientation=Horizontal.
- [high|missing-behavior] VSWG has no occupancy-map packing — RowSpan tiles leave permanent holes — ours: greedy per-row packing; next row starts below the tallest tile, cells beside tall tiles never reused (VariableSizedWrapGrid.cs:32-44, :59-73) vs WinUI: FindNextAvailableRectInternal scans cell-by-cell skipping occupied, back-fills beside/below multi-span tiles; spans clamp to remaining columns (VariableSizedWrapGrid_OccupancyMap.cpp:449-505, :462-464). Fix: 2D occupancy grid — place each tile in the first free rowSpan×colSpan rect, children absolutely positioned at cell*index.
- [high|engine-gap] Viewbox does not affect layout size — ours: scale is composited ScaleX/ScaleY only, siblings reserve the UNSCALED size; a 1.8x Viewbox (LayoutMiscPages.cs:73) paints over neighbors (Viewbox.cs:15-19, :64-77) vs WinUI: MeasureOverride desiredSize = scale * childDesiredSize; Arrange recomputes scale from finalSize (Viewbox.cpp:284-289, :316-334). Fix: add a measure-override/scale-aware layout seam so Viewbox reports scale*childDesired. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Canvas clips children; WinUI Canvas does not — ours: ClipToBounds = true (Canvas.cs:35, doc at :12) vs WinUI: "Canvas doesn't clip to its bounds typically" (canvas.cpp:80-93). Fix: default ClipToBounds = false; optional clip parameter. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-api] No Canvas.ZIndex — ours: CanvasChild is (X, Y, Child) only (Canvas.cs:7; no ZIndex in src/) vs WinUI: Canvas_ZIndex → OnZOrderChanged re-sorts render order (uielement.cpp:2797-2800). Fix: `int ZIndex = 0` on CanvasChild; stable-sort wrappers by ZIndex.
- [medium|missing-api] VSWG missing ItemWidth/ItemHeight (first-item fallback), MaximumRowsOrColumns, children alignment — ours: only fixed cell=60, columns=4 (VariableSizedWrapGrid.cs:20) vs WinUI: NaN ItemWidth/Height → first item's DesiredSize; MaximumRowsOrColumns clamps itemsPerLine; Horizontal/VerticalChildrenAlignment offsets via ComputeAlignmentOffsets (Partial.cpp:113-147, :265, :290-293, :525-584). Fix: add itemWidth/itemHeight (default first tile's natural size), maximumRowsOrColumns clamp, alignment offsets.
- [medium|bug] Viewbox scale math wrong when one axis is unconstrained — ours: ComputeAxis returns 1 for an infinite axis, then Min/Max over that 1 — Uniform with infinite width and scaleY=2 yields 1; UniformToFill with scaleY=0.5 yields 1; content<=0 yields 1 (Viewbox.cs:54-55, :42-43) vs WinUI: constrained axis's scale copied onto the unconstrained axis BEFORE the stretch switch; content≈0 gives scale 0 (Viewbox.cpp:102-109, :96-97). Fix: if availableWidth infinite set sx=sy (and vice versa) before the switch; return 0 for content<=0. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Viewbox UniformToFill overflow center-anchored + unclipped vs WinUI top-left + clipped — ours: child centered, transform origin defaults (0.5,0.5), no ClipToBounds — overflow spills all four sides (Viewbox.cs:64-66; Element.cs:141) vs WinUI: container arranged at (0,0), CScaleTransform center 0,0 — overflow right/bottom only, layout-clipped (Viewbox.cpp:325-331). Fix: UniformToFill/None → TransformOrigin 0,0, Justify/Align Start, ClipToBounds on the outer box.
- [medium|engine-gap] Interactive content inside a Viewbox hit-tests at unscaled rects — ours: hit walk applies only LocalTransform.Dx/Dy; zero 'Scale' matches in InputDispatcher.cs (InputDispatcher.cs:1023, :1046; Viewbox.cs:71-73) vs WinUI: pointer coords transformed through render transforms — scaled Button clickable at its visual location (Viewbox.cpp:19-22). Fix: include accumulated ScaleX/ScaleY (about origin) in InputDispatcher.Hit/HitAny. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-api] RelativePanel missing Padding/BorderBrush/BorderThickness/CornerRadius/BackgroundSizing — ours: only width/height/children (RelativePanel.cs:19-44) vs WinUI: measure subtracts HelperGetCombinedThickness; full border/padding getters (RelativePanel.cpp:22-27, :111-166). Fix: optional padding/border/corner params on the outer BoxEl, subtracted from the child area.
- [low|missing-behavior] VSWG over-span tile overflows unclamped — ours: ColSpan > columns gets a full span*cell row, overflowing the panel (VariableSizedWrapGrid.cs:32, :67) vs WinUI: columnSpan clamped to remaining map columns; first-line rects min'd to finalSize (OccupancyMap.cpp:462-464; Partial.cpp:387-407). Fix: clamp span to min(span, columns − used). (QUICK)
- [low|missing-behavior] Border background extends under the border; WinUI default InnerBorderEdge insets it — ours: BoxEl Fill covers the full rect with the ring stroked inside on top (BorderControl.cs:18-25; SceneRecorder.cs:676, :656-657 inset bw*0.5) vs WinUI: default BackgroundSizing != OuterBorderEdge deflates the background by borderThickness so translucent strokes composite over the backdrop (Border.cpp:552-571). Fix: deflate fill geometry by BorderWidth when bordered (or add BackgroundSizing defaulting InnerBorderEdge). (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-api] Border factory bakes card-chrome defaults; a bare WinUI Border is inexpressible — ours: defaults borderWidth=1, cornerRadius=8, padding=12; null borderColor/background coalesce to Tok.StrokeCardDefault/Tok.FillCardDefault (BorderControl.cs:13-24) vs WinUI: no implicit chrome; default brushes null (Border.cpp:216-252, :439-447). Fix: null = transparent/omit; default width/corner/padding 0; card look behind an explicit preset.

**Do it better**
- [low|improvement] Opt-in rounded-corner child clip on Border (WinUI pain point) — WinUI CornerRadius never clips content, devs hand-roll clips (Border.cpp:261-285; hit-testing only honors corners, :765-806); we already have ClipToBounds (Element.cs:178) honored in the hit walk (InputDispatcher.cs:1025). Fix: add `clipChild` parameter setting ClipToBounds with the corner radius — one-line win for media/thumbnail cards.

### Text display (RichTextBlock / TextEl / type ramp)

- [high|bug] TextEl default Color hardcoded #E6E6E6 — not theme-bound, wrong in both themes — ours: `Color = ColorF.FromRgba(0xE6,0xE6,0xE6)` (src/FluentGpu.Dsl/Element.cs:303) vs WinUI: default = DefaultTextForegroundThemeBrush = SystemBaseHighColor; TextFillColorPrimary = #FFFFFF dark / #E4000000 light (generic.xaml:1101; Common_themeresources_any.xaml:5, :209 — our Tok matches, Tokens.cs:330, :418). Fix: default TextEl color to Tok.TextPrimary (resolved at record time). (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-behavior] No text selection on display text — ours: "no input or selection"; selection rects render only for text-EDIT nodes (RichTextBlock.cs:9; SceneRecorder.cs:339-345) vs WinUI: IsTextSelectionEnabled=TRUE by default on CRichTextBlock; get_SelectedText; TextBlock opt-in (RichTextBlock.cpp:1730; RichTextBlock.g.h:102; TextBlock.cpp:583). Fix: IsTextSelectionEnabled on TextEl/RichTextBlock reusing the TextEditStyle selection-rect path (read-only, no caret); default true for RichTextBlock, false for TextEl; IBeam cursor while selectable. (ENGINE)
- [medium|styling-delta] RichTextBlock invents 560px MaxWidth cap + fixed 10px paragraph gap — ours: MaxWidth = 560, Gap = 10 in Create and Article (RichTextBlock.cs:26, :45, :25, :44) vs WinUI: fills its given width; BaseRichTextBlockStyle sets only font/wrap/trim (generic.xaml:13286-13295); paragraph spacing is app-set Paragraph margins. - [medium|engine-gap] Bold bit renders 700; the whole WinUI ramp is SemiBold 600 — ours: `bold ? DWRITE_FONT_WEIGHT_BOLD : NORMAL` (src/FluentGpu.Rhi.D3D12/GlyphRenderer.cs:231; Typography.cs:8-9 self-documents) vs WinUI: BaseTextBlockStyle FontWeight=SemiBold inherited by BodyStrong/Subtitle/Title/TitleLarge/Display (TextBlock_themeresources.xaml:13, :26, :36, :40, :44, :48). Fix: numeric FontWeight on TextEl (at least SemiBold); map ramp factories to 600. This is THE shared engine item gating bar-10/ttip-title-01/cd-13/pp-03. (ENGINE)
- [medium|bug] Duplicate disagreeing ramps: TextBlocks.Subtitle Regular vs Ui.Subtitle/WinUI SemiBold — ours: TextBlockDemo.cs:16 Bold=false vs Typography.cs:17 Bold=true; gallery uses the wrong one (MiscPages.cs:40) vs WinUI: SubtitleTextBlockStyle inherits SemiBold (TextBlock_themeresources.xaml:36-39, :13). Fix: TextBlocks.Subtitle Bold=true; better, delete TextBlocks and forward to the Ui.* ramp. (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] Caption uses secondary foreground; WinUI keeps primary — ours: Caption Color = Tok.TextSecondary (Typography.cs:13; TextBlockDemo.cs:25) vs WinUI: CaptionTextBlockStyle sets only FontSize 12 + Normal — default TextFillColorPrimary (TextBlock_themeresources.xaml:19-22). Fix: Caption → Tok.TextPrimary; opt into secondary via .Secondary() (Typography.cs:28). (QUICK)
- [medium|styling-delta] Ramp factories miss Wrap + CharacterEllipsis defaults — ours: only Ui.Body/BodyLarge set Wrap (Typography.cs:14, :16); rest default NoWrap + Trim=None (Element.cs:327-329); engine DOES implement trimming (TextLayoutEngine.cs:191, :277; LineBreaker.cs:40-101) vs WinUI: BaseTextBlockStyle TextTrimming=CharacterEllipsis, TextWrapping=Wrap inherited by every ramp (TextBlock_themeresources.xaml:14-15). Fix: set Wrap=TextWrap.Wrap + Trim=TextTrim.CharacterEllipsis on every Ui.* and TextBlocks.* factory. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-api] No LineHeight / LineStackingStrategy / TextLineBounds — ours: line height fixed at (Asc+Desc)*scale, fallback size*1.3 (TextLayoutEngine.cs:136-137; no prop on Element.cs:293-346) vs WinUI: LineHeight + LineStackingStrategy (TextBlock.g.h:89-92); BaseTextBlockStyle LineStackingStrategy=MaxHeight, TextLineBounds=Full (TextBlock_themeresources.xaml:16-17); NOTE the 16/20/…/92 spec figures have NO LineHeight setters in WinUI XAML — they come from font metrics. Fix: TextEl.LineHeight (DIP, 0=auto) through TextLayoutEngine; optional BlockLineHeight mode. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-api] No TextAlignment, FontStyle (italic), CharacterSpacing — ours: absent; LTR design-advance positioning (GlyphRenderer.cs:53) vs WinUI: get_TextAlignment, get_FontStyle, get_CharacterSpacing (TextBlock.g.h:108, :72, :62). Fix: TextAlignment as line-level x-offset in EmitLine (cheap); italic via DWRITE_FONT_STYLE_ITALIC in face resolution; CharacterSpacing lower priority. (ENGINE)
- [low|missing-api] RichTextBlock lacks OverflowContentTarget, TextHighlighters, TextIndent — ours: only Trim/MaxLines (Element.cs:329-331) vs WinUI: RichTextBlock.g.h:98, :113, :114. Fix: defer overflow flow-linking; TextHighlighters-style range highlight reusing selection rects; TextIndent in LineBreaker. (ENGINE)

**Effort:** InfoBar/InfoBadge **M** · TeachingTip/ToolTip **L** · ContentDialog **M** · Progress **M** · Expander **M** · SplitView **L** (near-rewrite: modes+motion+dismiss+events) · Flyout-infra **L** · Media **L** (M for chrome-only, L with pipeline) · PersonPicture **S** · Icons/AnimatedIcon **M** · Panels **L** (RPGraph + occupancy map + 3 engine seams) · Text-display **L**.
Land the cross-cutting ENGINE items first — numeric FontWeight 600 (unblocks 5 controls), measure-override seam (bar-01, vb-02, rp-01), scale-aware hit-testing (vb-04), TryGetTrackValue (exp-08) — then the ~20 (QUICK) one-liners (cursors, defaults, token fixes) in one batch.

## engine-systemic

This group covers five cross-cutting audits (cursors, tokens, motion, focus, missing controls) plus the consolidated engine backlog from every other control group. The two highest-leverage fixes in the whole parity effort live here: the Reconciler Hand-cursor default (engine-01, heals 36 findings with one deleted line) and the light-theme elevation-gradient flip (tok-elev-flip-01, affects every bordered control).

### cursor-audit

> **LANDED 2026-06-11 (Wave A):** engine-01 and engine-02 are implemented - the reconciler no longer defaults
> clickables to Hand, and an explicit `Cursor` (Arrow included) sets `CursorBit` and terminates the hover walk.
> Every per-control "Fix: add `Cursor = CursorId.Arrow`" in this document is therefore OBSOLETE and must NOT be
> applied - post-CursorBit it would wrongly mask ancestor cursors WinUI never masks. The only explicit cursors that
> remain correct: HyperlinkButton Hand, EditableText root I-beam, EditableText.InnerButton Arrow, NumberBox SpinCell Arrow.

- [high|engine-gap] Engine default gives every OnClick element a Hand cursor (root cause) — ours: `ii.Cursor = CursorId.Hand;` whenever `b.OnClick is not null` (src/FluentGpu.Reconciler/Reconciler.cs:1001; explicit overrides only at :1106; resolution walk src/FluentGpu.Input/InputDispatcher.cs:642-654) vs WinUI: the ONLY control Hand is HyperLinkButton_Partial.cpp:32 `SetCursor(MouseCursorHand)` + inline text hyperlinks (TextBlock.cpp:3488, RichTextBlock.cpp:2995); controls/dev sets no cursors except WebView2 forwarding (WebView2.cpp:724-773). Fix: delete the Hand default at Reconciler.cs:1001 (leave Arrow/unset). Hand stays opt-in — HyperlinkButton.cs:126 already Hand, EditableText.cs:378 already IBeam; the Arrow opt-outs at Button.cs:178, IconButton.cs:99, RepeatButton.cs:112, ToggleButton.cs:166 become redundant (harmless). (ENGINE) (QUICK)
- [high|bug] Explicit Arrow cannot mask an ancestor IBeam/Hand — Arrow doubles as the "unset" sentinel — ours: InteractionInfo.Cursor non-nullable (src/FluentGpu.Scene/Columns.cs:265); InputDispatcher.cs:649 skips Cursor==Arrow and keeps walking, so TextBox DeleteButton / PasswordBox eye (Cursor=Arrow, EditableText.cs:426) inside the IBeam root (EditableText.cs:378) resolve to IBeam vs WinUI: forces Arrow on exactly these inner buttons — TextBox_Partial.cpp:884, PasswordBox_Partial.cpp:571, AutoSuggestBox_Partial.cpp:807. Fix: store explicit-cursor presence (HandlerMask bit or 0xFF=unset sentinel) so explicit Arrow terminates the walk in InputDispatcher.UpdateCursor. Survives the engine-01 flip. (ENGINE)
- [high|bug] ToolTip wrapper turns ANY tooltipped element into a Hand-cursored tab stop — ours: `OnClick = Toggle` on the target wrapper, no TabStop=false (ToolTip.cs:236) → inherits Hand (Reconciler:1001) + auto-Focusable (Reconciler:1111) vs WinUI: ToolTipService adds no click handler; press dismisses (we already do via OnPointerPressed = OnPressed, ToolTip.cs:234). Fix: drop the legacy OnClick=Toggle (or TabStop=false + Cursor=Arrow if click-toggle compat must stay). (QUICK)
- [high|styling-delta] NavigationView: every interactive surface shows Hand (user-reported) — ours: no Cursor anywhere in NavigationView.cs; raw OnClick at :810 pane toggle, :738 top items, :961 left rows, :674 overflow, :637 overlay rows, :378 scrim vs WinUI: no SetCursor in NavigationView sources → arrow. Fix: self-heals via engine-01; interim Cursor=CursorId.Arrow on all six sites. (QUICK)
- [high|styling-delta] OverlayHost scrim: Hand over the entire window while any flyout/menu/dialog is open — ours: scrim OnClick with no Cursor (OverlayHost.cs:782) vs WinUI: dismiss layer never changes the cursor. Fix: self-heals via engine-01; interim Cursor=Arrow on the scrim. (QUICK)
- [high|styling-delta] AutoSuggestBox query button + suggestion rows show Hand; WinUI explicitly forces Arrow on the query button — ours: AutoSuggestBox.cs:376/:384 query OnClick=SubmitQuery, :504/:508 rows; query button also hits engine-02 (Arrow can't mask field IBeam) vs WinUI: AutoSuggestBox_Partial.cpp:807 `SetCursor(MouseCursorArrow)` on m_tpTextBoxQueryButtonPart. Fix: engine-01 + engine-02; interim Cursor=Arrow on both. (QUICK)
- [high|styling-delta] Slider track/thumb shows Hand whenever the value tooltip is enabled (the default) — ours: Slider.cs:755/:780 `OnClick = tooltipEnabled ? CloseTip : null`, IsThumbToolTipEnabled defaults true (Slider.cs:142) vs WinUI: no SetCursor in Slider sources → arrow. Fix: self-heals via engine-01, no local change needed. (QUICK)

### motion-audit

- [medium|motion-delta] SelectorBar selection pill has no ScaleX grow/shrink — ours: pill static 16px, Fill swap transparent↔accent only (SelectorBar.cs:36-43; :32-35 admits "engine has no per-item ScaleX state machine") vs WinUI: PillTransform ScaleX→4 SplineDoubleKeyFrame KeySpline 0,0,0,1 over ComboBoxItemScaleAnimationDuration=167ms (SelectorBar.xaml:108-112; ComboBox_themeresources.xaml:330). Fix: mount the pill only when selected with LayoutTransition(Opacity, Tween(167f, Easing.FluentPopOpen), Enter:(Sx:0.25, Opacity:0), Exit same) — the primitive ListView.cs:358-361 already uses. (QUICK)
- [medium|missing-behavior] PipsPager: no MaxVisiblePips viewport, no animated scroll-to-center, no nav buttons — ours: static strip of all dots, zero animation code (PipsPager.cs:18-63) vs WinUI: ScrollToCenterOfViewport via BringIntoViewOptions AlignmentRatio 0.5 + AnimationDesired(true) (PipsPager.cpp:240-253); prev/next glyphs EDDB/EDDC FontSize 8 (PipsPager_themeresources.xaml:102-106). Fix: MaxVisiblePips clipped viewport + animated strip translate centering the selected pip (~250ms FluentDecelerate) + EDDB/EDDC repeat nav buttons.
- [low|motion-delta] ComboBox item pill missing SelectedPressed ScaleY shrink (consts declared but dead) — ours: pill BoxEl has no PressScale (ComboBox.cs:771); ItemPillScaleMin=0.625 / PillScaleMs=167 (ComboBox.cs:79-80) referenced nowhere vs WinUI: SelectedPressed PillTransform ScaleY→ComboBoxItemPillMinScale over 167ms KeySpline 0,0,0,1 (ComboBox_themeresources.xaml:726-727). Fix: PressScale = ComboBox.ItemPillScaleMin, PressDurationMs = ComboBox.PillScaleMs, PressEasing = Easing.FluentPopOpen. (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] ItemContainer fades use FluentDecelerate where WinUI says KeySpline 0,0,0,1 — ours: ItemContainer.cs:115/:144 Tween(167f, Easing.FluentDecelerate) (0.1,0.9,0.2,1 — Foundation/Easing.cs:76); own comments at :103-104/:133-134 cite 0,0,0,1 vs WinUI: SplineDoubleKeyFrame Opacity KeySpline="0,0,0,1" at ControlFastAnimationDuration (ItemContainer.xaml:54-55, 73-74, 95-96). Fix: Easing.FluentPopOpen at ItemContainer only — Repeater.cs:78 is EXCLUDED (corrected): its WinUI counterpart uses a LINEAR fade at DefaultAnimationDuration=250ms and cubic (0.55,0)(0,1)/(1,0)(1,1) scale curves (LinedFlowLayoutItemCollectionTransitionProvider.cpp:257-261, 363-377 + .h:51-52). (QUICK)
- [low|motion-delta] ListView/TreeView selection-pill spring ~2x slower than WinUI's 167ms reveal; opacity not 83ms linear — ours: spring(0.30, 0.85) drives Sy 0→1 AND opacity, ≈300ms+ settle (ListView.cs:358-361; TreeView.cs:493) vs WinUI: opacity 83ms linear + ScaleY over 167ms cubic(0.167,0.167)(0,1) (ListViewBaseItemPresenter_Partial.cpp:946-983). Fix: spring substitution is blessed; tighten response to ~0.17-0.20 (MotionSprings.PartSettle) for scale, keep fade ≈83ms.
- [low|motion-delta] NavigationView pill: 600ms stretch-between-items choreography not expressed (slide-only spring) — ours: UseSpring TranslateY (NavPill 0.30/0.85) + 150ms EaseOut opacity, no scale deformation (NavigationView.cs:1015-1016) vs WinUI: 600ms — scale stretches to span |to−from| at 33% via (0.9,0.1)(1.0,0.2), settles via (0.1,0.9)(0.2,1.0); position single-frame-steps at 33%; CenterPoint anim 200ms (NavigationView.cpp:1990-1993, 2205-2221). Fix: spring slide is intentional; add a transient ScaleY stretch keyframe pair (grow toward target, settle) alongside the spring.
- [low|motion-delta] CheckBox uncheck is instant; WinUI plays ~68ms NormalOnToNormalOff — ours: uncheck swaps markChildren to [] with no Exit transition (CheckBox.cs:106-110) vs WinUI: markers 0.0→0.0253125 of 2666.67ms ≈ 67.5ms (AnimatedAcceptVisualSource.cpp:1945-1946, :105). Fix: give the mark mount an Exit leg (~68ms opacity or trim retract).
- [low|motion-delta] Indeterminate dash 200ms draw-on has no WinUI source — ours: DrawnDash DurationMs=200f StrokeTrimEnd reveal, no citation (CheckBox.cs:238, keyframes :243-244) vs WinUI: NormalIndeterminate is a single held-frame marker, value 0.9690625 at AnimatedAcceptVisualSource.cpp:1981 (corrected from :1982), no draw-on segment exists. - [low|engine-gap] No per-direction state durations: WinUI returns-to-Normal faster than it enters hover/press — ours: single HoverEasing/PressEasing + one HoverDurationMs/PressDurationMs (Element.cs:151-152); Slider.cs:251 uses 250f both ways vs WinUI: Normal-return = ControlFastAnimationDuration 167ms vs PointerOver/Pressed = 250ms, all KeySpline 0,0,0,1 (Slider_themeresources.xaml:207-215, :219-239). ### focus-audit

- [high|engine-gap] ListView/GridView: every item is a Tab stop; WinUI list is ONE stop (TabNavigation=Once) — ours: each item Focusable=true (ListView.cs:379-380); MoveFocus flat-walks all focusables (InputDispatcher.cs:814-825); no TabNavigation/Once concept in src/FluentGpu.Input vs WinUI: ListView style `<Setter Property="TabNavigation" Value="Once" />` (generic.xaml:9286). - [medium|styling-delta] Reconciler default FocusVisualMargin is -3; WinUI property default is 0 — ours: `ii.FocusVisualMargin = b.FocusVisualMargin ?? Edges4.All(-3f)` (Reconciler.cs:1113; Element.cs:119-121 doc repeats it) vs WinUI: FrameworkElement_FocusVisualMargin default = (0,0,0,0) (DependencyProperty.cpp:410-413); only button-family templates SET -3. Fix: default null to Edges4.All(0); set -3 explicitly where WinUI does (already correct in Button/Toggle/Repeat/Hyperlink/AppBar/MenuBar/GridView). Root cause of findings focus-02..07. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-api] TextBox shows dual focus ring; WinUI disables system focus visuals — ours: EditableText.cs:376 root Focusable=IsEnabled; engine rings any FocusVisual node (SceneRecorder.cs:476); no UseSystemFocusVisuals on BoxEl (Element.cs:113-123) → Tab shows ring + accent underline (EditableText.cs:338-343) vs WinUI: `UseSystemFocusVisuals={ThemeResource IsApplicationFocusVisualKindReveal}` (false under default HighVisibility) — fill + 2px accent underline only, NO ring (TextBox_themeresources.xaml:195). - [medium|missing-behavior] Programmatic focus never shows the ring even in keyboard mode — ours: FocusTrap entry calls hooks.FocusNode(firstStop, false) unconditionally (OverlayHost.cs:606); no last-input-device tracking (InputDispatcher.cs:915 caller-chosen) vs WinUI: visual shows when FocusState==Keyboard OR (Programmatic AND last input Keyboard/GamepadOrRemote) (focusmgr.cpp:2786-2794). - [medium|styling-delta] NavigationViewItem ring 3px outside; WinUI hugs item bounds — ours: NavigationView.cs:960 row Focusable, no margin → -3 default; ring radius grows 8→11 vs WinUI: no FocusVisualMargin on NVI (only TogglePaneButton=0 NavigationView.xaml:197, PaneSearchButton=-4,0 NavigationView_themeresources.xaml:344) → default 0. Fix: widen icon slots (NavItem, TabView, MenuFlyout) to accept Element so an ImageEl thumbnail works — WaveeMusic's sidebar shows playlist/album cover thumbnails.
- [medium|missing-api] WebView2 absent (nice-to-have) — ours: no hit vs WinUI: controls/dev/WebView2/ full folder. Fix: composition-hosted WebView2 island for OAuth/web content; WaveeMusic can use system-browser loopback auth — only build if embedded login is required. (ENGINE)
- [medium|missing-behavior] Frame-style page transitions absent — ours: Navigation.cs:73-85 PageHost swaps the route subtree with no transition vs WinUI: Frame_Partial.h:132-141 GoBackWithTransitionInfoImpl/NavigateImpl take NavigationTransitionInfo (entrance/drill-in/slide). Fix: optional entrance/drill-in in PageHost on Push/Pop via existing UseTransition/UseKeyframes (167-250ms fade+translate); pure component work. (QUICK)
- [low|missing-api] Explicit skips (merged) — PullToRefresh (RefreshContainer.idl:18-26; touch gesture, desktop client refreshes via data push), TwoPaneView (TwoPaneView.idl:43-50; flex rows + SplitView.cs cover it), PagerControl (PagerControl.idl:45-74; lists are virtualized via VirtualLayout.cs, PipsPager covers dots), SemanticZoom (SemanticZoom_Partial.h:5-6,37-41; AnnotatedScrollBar.cs is the modern answer), ListBox (ListBox_Partial.h:12-14; ListView + ComboBox dropdown subsume), Hub (Hub_Partial.cpp; WaveeShell.cs already does ScrollEl + section rows), RichEditBox (RichEditBox_Partial.cpp; plain editing suffices), MonochromaticOverlayPresenter (internal XAML ColorPicker helper), InkCanvas/InkToolBar/MapControl (no inking/maps), LayoutPanel (LayoutPanel.idl:8-13; Repeater + IVirtualLayout seam, VirtualLayout.cs:15-25, already gives attached-layout composition), AppBarElementContainer (AppBarElementContainer_Partial.cpp) — skip stands, but corrected rationale: CommandBar.Create takes IReadOnlyList<AppBarCommand> (CommandBar.cs:85-90; AppBarCommand record at CommandBarFlyout.cs:22-28), NOT arbitrary Elements; the skip only holds because the element model lets apps hand-build custom toolbar rows.

**Do it better**
- [low|improvement] Our Navigator beats WinUI Frame — keep and document — ours: back stack is serializable typed state (Navigation.cs:15-65, Serialize/Deserialize for deep links/cold-launch restore); pages keep state by reconciler identity vs WinUI: transient page cache (InitialTransientCacheSize, Frame_Partial.h:26-28) — corrected: Frame DOES have GetNavigationStateImpl/SetNavigationStateImpl (Frame_Partial.h:162-166), so the improvement is narrower: typed Route records vs an opaque HSTRING blob whose page parameters must be serialization-primitive types. Fix: no change; add ft-01 transitions on top.

### Engine work items (deduplicated, all control groups)

Each item is one distinct engine capability; controls that need it in parentheses.

1. **Remove OnClick→Hand cursor default** — Reconciler.cs:1001 (heals 36 cursor findings across every clickable control). (QUICK)
2. **Explicit-cursor presence sentinel** so Arrow masks ancestor IBeam/Hand — Columns.cs:265 + InputDispatcher.cs:649 (TextBox delete, PasswordBox eye, AutoSuggestBox query button).
3. **Key-activation parity in InputDispatcher** — Enter: pressed-visual on down, click on key-UP (bb-01, InputDispatcher.cs:724-728 vs ButtonBaseKeyProcess.h:51/:110-113); IsRepeat guard for ALL clickables INCLUDING RepeatButton (bb-02 corrected — WinUI's held Enter yields exactly one click even on RepeatButton, RepeatButton_Partial.cpp:212-217 arms the timer for Space only); any-key-down cancels an armed Space/Enter press (bb-05, ButtonBaseKeyProcess.h:64-70). (All clickables.)
4. **AcceptsReturn/ActivateOnEnter per-node opt-out** honored at InputDispatcher.cs:724 (CheckBox CheckBox_Partial.cpp:27, RadioButton RadioButton_Partial.cpp:30, ToggleSwitch ToggleSwitch_Partial.cpp:1002-1007).
5. **Pressed visual tracks pointer during hold** — re-evaluate Pressed on PointerMove vs _down bounds (bb-03, ButtonBase_Partial.cpp:629-638). (All buttons.)
6. **Pointer focus on press, not release** — InputDispatcher.cs:282-283 vs ButtonBase_Partial.cpp:700-709 (bb-06); plus **AllowFocusOnInteraction analogue** — skip pointer-focus, keep tab-focus (ib-02, AppBarButton_themeresources.xaml:136; IconButton).
7. **ClickMode (Press/Hover) API or document release-only** (bb-04, low/optional).
8. **Pointer-cancel/exit delivery to the captured OnDrag target** — InputDispatcher.cs:339-350 CancelPointer is silent (rating-cancel-01; RatingControl alt-tab mid-sweep leaks downRef). Note: ts-drag-exit-01 was CORRECTED to control-side only — implicit capture already delivers outside releases (InputDispatcher.cs:185-188, :287-301); ToggleSwitch fix is in Exit() gating on g.Moved.
9. **Middle-button routing** — InputDispatcher.cs:203 blocks non-left, :223 hardcodes Button=0; PointerEventArgs.Button=2 exists (Events.cs:61) (TabView middle-click close, TabViewItem.cpp:418-462).
10. **Touch input generation + device-kind on hover paths** — corrected: PointerKind {Mouse,Touch,Pen} EXISTS (Events.cs:16, Pal.cs:26, InputDispatcher.cs:223; RatingControl.cs:243 already branches) but the Win32 pump never emits Touch (no WM_POINTER/WM_TOUCH in src/FluentGpu.Windows/Pal/) and hover is set ungated (InputDispatcher.cs:178) (Slider touch behaviors, RatingControl).

(RepeatButton, ScrollBar arrows, NumberBox spinners, DatePicker spin.)

SemiLight 350 + CharacterSpacing -25, InfoBar bar-10, TeachingTip ttip-title-01 14px SemiBold, ContentDialog cd-13, AnnotatedScrollBar asb-weight-04, entire type ramp).
